	IM_CMVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_CMVV_VVM_npt[1,IM_CMVV_state], IM_CMVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IM_CMVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CMVV_VVL_npt[2,IM_CMVV_state],2)
	IM_CMVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_CMVV_VVL_npt[1,IM_CMVV_state], IM_CMVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Reviews and Audits V&V
	IM_RaAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RaAVV_VVH_npt[2,IM_RaAVV_state],2)
	IM_RaAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_RaAVV_VVH_npt[1,IM_RaAVV_state], IM_RaAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	IM_RaAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RaAVV_VVM_npt[2,IM_RaAVV_state],2)
	IM_RaAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_RaAVV_VVM_npt[1,IM_RaAVV_state], IM_RaAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IM_RaAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RaAVV_VVL_npt[2,IM_RaAVV_state],2)
	IM_RaAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_RaAVV_VVL_npt[1,IM_RaAVV_state], IM_RaAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Implementation Phase Activity Summary Report Generation
	IM_VVASRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVASRG_VVH_npt[2,IM_VVASRG_state],2)
	IM_VVASRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVASRG_VVH_npt[1,IM_VVASRG_state], IM_VVASRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	IM_VVASRG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVASRG_VVM_npt[2,IM_VVASRG_state],2)
	IM_VVASRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVASRG_VVM_npt[1,IM_VVASRG_state], IM_VVASRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IM_VVASRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVASRG_VVL_npt[2,IM_VVASRG_state],2)
	IM_VVASRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVASRG_VVL_npt[1,IM_VVASRG_state], IM_VVASRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(VV=H)P(attribute states|VV=H)
	# m2 = P(VV=M)P(attribute states|VV=M)
	# m3 = P(VV=L)P(attribute states|VV=L)

	IM_VV_m1 <- IM_VVH_prior * IM_SCaSCDE_VVH_like * IM_IAVV_VVH_like * IM_TAVV_VVH_like * IM_CAVV_VVH_like * IM_HAVV_VVH_like * IM_SAVV_VVH_like * IM_RAVV_VVH_like * IM_VVSCTCG_VVH_like * IM_VVSITCG_VVH_like * IM_VVSQTCG_VVH_like * IM_VVSATCG_VVH_like * IM_VVSCTPG_VVH_like * IM_VVSITPG_VVH_like * IM_VVSQTPG_VVH_like * IM_VVSCTE_VVH_like * IM_CMVV_VVH_like * IM_RaAVV_VVH_like * IM_VVASRG_VVH_like
	IM_VV_m2 <- IM_VVM_prior * IM_SCaSCDE_VVM_like * IM_IAVV_VVM_like * IM_TAVV_VVM_like * IM_CAVV_VVM_like * IM_HAVV_VVM_like * IM_SAVV_VVM_like * IM_RAVV_VVM_like * IM_VVSCTCG_VVM_like * IM_VVSITCG_VVM_like * IM_VVSQTCG_VVM_like * IM_VVSATCG_VVM_like * IM_VVSCTPG_VVM_like * IM_VVSITPG_VVM_like * IM_VVSQTPG_VVM_like * IM_VVSCTE_VVM_like * IM_CMVV_VVM_like * IM_RaAVV_VVM_like * IM_VVASRG_VVM_like
	IM_VV_m3 <- IM_VVL_prior * IM_SCaSCDE_VVL_like * IM_IAVV_VVL_like * IM_TAVV_VVL_like * IM_CAVV_VVL_like * IM_HAVV_VVL_like * IM_SAVV_VVL_like * IM_RAVV_VVL_like * IM_VVSCTCG_VVL_like * IM_VVSITCG_VVL_like * IM_VVSQTCG_VVL_like * IM_VVSATCG_VVL_like * IM_VVSCTPG_VVL_like * IM_VVSITPG_VVL_like * IM_VVSQTPG_VVL_like * IM_VVSCTE_VVL_like * IM_CMVV_VVL_like * IM_RaAVV_VVL_like * IM_VVASRG_VVL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	IM_VV_k <- 1 / (IM_VV_m1 + IM_VV_m2 + IM_VV_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in IM phase
	IM_VVH_post <- IM_VV_k * IM_VV_m1
	IM_VVM_post <- IM_VV_k * IM_VV_m2
	IM_VVL_post <- IM_VV_k * IM_VV_m3


	# Submodel - Implementation phase

	IM_Defect_passed_from_SD <- SD_Total_Remained_Defect

	# Defect Density likelihood: P(Defect Density|state of Dev quality)
	IM_DevH_DD_like ~ dgamma(2.5989,3.3317)
	IM_DevM_DD_like ~ dgamma(3.1588,3.1963)
	IM_DevL_DD_like ~ dgamma(3.3807,3.1969)

	# Defect density: the integral of P(Dev)*P(Defect Density|Dev) dDev
	IM_Defect_Density <- (IM_DevH_post * IM_DevH_DD_like + IM_DevM_post * IM_DevM_DD_like + IM_DevL_post * IM_DevL_DD_like)

	IM_Defect_introduced_in_current <- IM_FP * IM_Defect_Density

	# Complexity: (FP >= 1000)? High: (FP >= 100)? Medium: Low
	IM_Complexity <- step(IM_FP-1000)+(1-step(IM_FP-1000))*step(IM_FP-100)*2+step(99-IM_FP)*3

	# Defect Detection Probability (current) likelihood: P(DDP_current|state of VV quality)
	IM_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,IM_Complexity],IM_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,IM_Complexity])
	IM_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,IM_Complexity],IM_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,IM_Complexity])
	IM_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,IM_Complexity],IM_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,IM_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (current): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	IM_Defect_Detection_Probability_current <- IM_VVH_post * IM_VVH_DDP_current_like + IM_VVM_post * IM_VVM_DDP_current_like + IM_VVL_post * IM_VVL_DDP_current_like

	IM_Detected_Defect_current <- IM_Defect_introduced_in_current * IM_Defect_Detection_Probability_current

	IM_Remaining_Defect_current <- IM_Defect_introduced_in_current - IM_Detected_Defect_current

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous) likelihood: P(DDP_previous|state of VV quality)
	IM_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,IM_Complexity],IM_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,IM_Complexity])
	IM_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,IM_Complexity],IM_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,IM_Complexity])
	IM_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,IM_Complexity],IM_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,IM_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	IM_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous <- IM_VVH_post * IM_VVH_DDP_previous_like + IM_VVM_post * IM_VVM_DDP_previous_like + IM_VVL_post * IM_VVL_DDP_previous_like

	IM_Detected_Defect_previous <- IM_Defect_passed_from_SD * IM_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous

	IM_Remaining_Defect_previous <- IM_Defect_passed_from_SD - IM_Detected_Defect_previous

	IM_Total_Remained_Defect <- IM_Remaining_Defect_current + IM_Remaining_Defect_previous


	# Dev Attribute model - Test phase

	# prior probability of Dev quality in ST phase
	ST_DevH_prior ~ dbeta(0.45, 1.29)
	ST_DevM_prior ~ dbeta(1.75, 1.19)
	ST_DevL_prior ~ dbeta(0.83, 5.42)

	# Attribute Software Integration Test Execution

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	ST_SITE_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SITE_DevH_npt[2,ST_SITE_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of Dev quality)
	ST_SITE_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SITE_DevH_npt[1,ST_SITE_state], ST_SITE_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SITE_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SITE_DevM_npt[2,ST_SITE_state],2)
	ST_SITE_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SITE_DevM_npt[1,ST_SITE_state], ST_SITE_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SITE_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SITE_DevL_npt[2,ST_SITE_state],2)
	ST_SITE_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SITE_DevL_npt[1,ST_SITE_state], ST_SITE_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Qualification Test Execution
	ST_SQTE_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SQTE_DevH_npt[2,ST_SQTE_state],2)
	ST_SQTE_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SQTE_DevH_npt[1,ST_SQTE_state], ST_SQTE_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SQTE_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SQTE_DevM_npt[2,ST_SQTE_state],2)
	ST_SQTE_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SQTE_DevM_npt[1,ST_SQTE_state], ST_SQTE_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SQTE_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SQTE_DevL_npt[2,ST_SQTE_state],2)
	ST_SQTE_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SQTE_DevL_npt[1,ST_SQTE_state], ST_SQTE_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Acceptance Procedure Generation
	ST_SAPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SAPG_DevH_npt[2,ST_SAPG_state],2)
	ST_SAPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SAPG_DevH_npt[1,ST_SAPG_state], ST_SAPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SAPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SAPG_DevM_npt[2,ST_SAPG_state],2)
	ST_SAPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SAPG_DevM_npt[1,ST_SAPG_state], ST_SAPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SAPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SAPG_DevL_npt[2,ST_SAPG_state],2)
	ST_SAPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SAPG_DevL_npt[1,ST_SAPG_state], ST_SAPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Acceptance Test Execution
	ST_SATE_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SATE_DevH_npt[2,ST_SATE_state],2)
	ST_SATE_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SATE_DevH_npt[1,ST_SATE_state], ST_SATE_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SATE_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SATE_DevM_npt[2,ST_SATE_state],2)
	ST_SATE_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SATE_DevM_npt[1,ST_SATE_state], ST_SATE_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SATE_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SATE_DevL_npt[2,ST_SATE_state],2)
	ST_SATE_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SATE_DevL_npt[1,ST_SATE_state], ST_SATE_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Traceability Analysis - Test Phase
	ST_TA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_TA_DevH_npt[2,ST_TA_state],2)
	ST_TA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_TA_DevH_npt[1,ST_TA_state], ST_TA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_TA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_TA_DevM_npt[2,ST_TA_state],2)
	ST_TA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_TA_DevM_npt[1,ST_TA_state], ST_TA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_TA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_TA_DevL_npt[2,ST_TA_state],2)
	ST_TA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_TA_DevL_npt[1,ST_TA_state], ST_TA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis - Test Phase
	ST_HA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_HA_DevH_npt[2,ST_HA_state],2)
	ST_HA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_HA_DevH_npt[1,ST_HA_state], ST_HA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_HA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_HA_DevM_npt[2,ST_HA_state],2)
	ST_HA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_HA_DevM_npt[1,ST_HA_state], ST_HA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_HA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_HA_DevL_npt[2,ST_HA_state],2)
	ST_HA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_HA_DevL_npt[1,ST_HA_state], ST_HA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis - Test Phase
	ST_SA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SA_DevH_npt[2,ST_SA_state],2)
	ST_SA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SA_DevH_npt[1,ST_SA_state], ST_SA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SA_DevM_npt[2,ST_SA_state],2)
	ST_SA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SA_DevM_npt[1,ST_SA_state], ST_SA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SA_DevL_npt[2,ST_SA_state],2)
	ST_SA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SA_DevL_npt[1,ST_SA_state], ST_SA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis - Test Phase
	ST_RA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RA_DevH_npt[2,ST_RA_state],2)
	ST_RA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_RA_DevH_npt[1,ST_RA_state], ST_RA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_RA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RA_DevM_npt[2,ST_RA_state],2)
	ST_RA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_RA_DevM_npt[1,ST_RA_state], ST_RA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_RA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RA_DevL_npt[2,ST_RA_state],2)
	ST_RA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_RA_DevL_npt[1,ST_RA_state], ST_RA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Configuration Management
	ST_CM_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_CM_DevH_npt[2,ST_CM_state],2)
	ST_CM_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_CM_DevH_npt[1,ST_CM_state], ST_CM_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_CM_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_CM_DevM_npt[2,ST_CM_state],2)
	ST_CM_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_CM_DevM_npt[1,ST_CM_state], ST_CM_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_CM_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_CM_DevL_npt[2,ST_CM_state],2)
	ST_CM_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_CM_DevL_npt[1,ST_CM_state], ST_CM_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Review and Audits
	ST_RaA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaA_DevH_npt[2,ST_RaA_state],2)
	ST_RaA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_RaA_DevH_npt[1,ST_RaA_state], ST_RaA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_RaA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaA_DevM_npt[2,ST_RaA_state],2)
	ST_RaA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_RaA_DevM_npt[1,ST_RaA_state], ST_RaA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_RaA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaA_DevL_npt[2,ST_RaA_state],2)
	ST_RaA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_RaA_DevL_npt[1,ST_RaA_state], ST_RaA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(Dev=H)P(attribute states|Dev=H)
	# m2 = P(Dev=M)P(attribute states|Dev=M)
	# m3 = P(Dev=L)P(attribute states|Dev=L)

	ST_Dev_m1 <- ST_DevH_prior * ST_SITE_DevH_like * ST_SQTE_DevH_like * ST_SAPG_DevH_like * ST_SATE_DevH_like * ST_TA_DevH_like * ST_HA_DevH_like * ST_SA_DevH_like * ST_RA_DevH_like * ST_CM_DevH_like * ST_RaA_DevH_like
	ST_Dev_m2 <- ST_DevM_prior * ST_SITE_DevM_like * ST_SQTE_DevM_like * ST_SAPG_DevM_like * ST_SATE_DevM_like * ST_TA_DevM_like * ST_HA_DevM_like * ST_SA_DevM_like * ST_RA_DevM_like * ST_CM_DevM_like * ST_RaA_DevM_like
	ST_Dev_m3 <- ST_DevL_prior * ST_SITE_DevL_like * ST_SQTE_DevL_like * ST_SAPG_DevL_like * ST_SATE_DevL_like * ST_TA_DevL_like * ST_HA_DevL_like * ST_SA_DevL_like * ST_RA_DevL_like * ST_CM_DevL_like * ST_RaA_DevL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	ST_Dev_k <- 1 / (ST_Dev_m1 + ST_Dev_m2 + ST_Dev_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in ST phase
	ST_DevH_post <- ST_Dev_k * ST_Dev_m1
	ST_DevM_post <- ST_Dev_k * ST_Dev_m2
	ST_DevL_post <- ST_Dev_k * ST_Dev_m3


	# V&V Attribute model - Test phase

	# prior probability of V&V quality in ST phase
	ST_VVH_prior ~ dbeta(0.45, 1.29)
	ST_VVM_prior ~ dbeta(1.75, 1.19)
	ST_VVL_prior ~ dbeta(0.83, 5.42)

	# Attribute V&V Software Integration Test Execution

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	ST_VVSITE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSITE_VVH_npt[2,ST_VVSITE_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of V&V quality)
	ST_VVSITE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSITE_VVH_npt[1,ST_VVSITE_state], ST_VVSITE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVSITE_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSITE_VVM_npt[2,ST_VVSITE_state],2)
	ST_VVSITE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSITE_VVM_npt[1,ST_VVSITE_state], ST_VVSITE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVSITE_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSITE_VVL_npt[2,ST_VVSITE_state],2)
	ST_VVSITE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSITE_VVL_npt[1,ST_VVSITE_state], ST_VVSITE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Qualification Test Execution
	ST_VVSQTE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSQTE_VVH_npt[2,ST_VVSQTE_state],2)
	ST_VVSQTE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSQTE_VVH_npt[1,ST_VVSQTE_state], ST_VVSQTE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVSQTE_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSQTE_VVM_npt[2,ST_VVSQTE_state],2)
	ST_VVSQTE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSQTE_VVM_npt[1,ST_VVSQTE_state], ST_VVSQTE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVSQTE_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSQTE_VVL_npt[2,ST_VVSQTE_state],2)
	ST_VVSQTE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSQTE_VVL_npt[1,ST_VVSQTE_state], ST_VVSQTE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Acceptance Procedure Generation
	ST_VVSAPG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSAPG_VVH_npt[2,ST_VVSAPG_state],2)
	ST_VVSAPG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSAPG_VVH_npt[1,ST_VVSAPG_state], ST_VVSAPG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVSAPG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSAPG_VVM_npt[2,ST_VVSAPG_state],2)
	ST_VVSAPG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSAPG_VVM_npt[1,ST_VVSAPG_state], ST_VVSAPG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVSAPG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSAPG_VVL_npt[2,ST_VVSAPG_state],2)
	ST_VVSAPG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSAPG_VVL_npt[1,ST_VVSAPG_state], ST_VVSAPG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Acceptance Test Execution
	ST_VVSATE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSATE_VVH_npt[2,ST_VVSATE_state],2)
	ST_VVSATE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSATE_VVH_npt[1,ST_VVSATE_state], ST_VVSATE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVSATE_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSATE_VVM_npt[2,ST_VVSATE_state],2)
	ST_VVSATE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSATE_VVM_npt[1,ST_VVSATE_state], ST_VVSATE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVSATE_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSATE_VVL_npt[2,ST_VVSATE_state],2)
	ST_VVSATE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSATE_VVL_npt[1,ST_VVSATE_state], ST_VVSATE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Traceability Analysis V&V - Test phase
	ST_TAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_TAVV_VVH_npt[2,ST_TAVV_state],2)
	ST_TAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_TAVV_VVH_npt[1,ST_TAVV_state], ST_TAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_TAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_TAVV_VVM_npt[2,ST_TAVV_state],2)
	ST_TAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_TAVV_VVM_npt[1,ST_TAVV_state], ST_TAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_TAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_TAVV_VVL_npt[2,ST_TAVV_state],2)
	ST_TAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_TAVV_VVL_npt[1,ST_TAVV_state], ST_TAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis V&V - Test phase
	ST_HAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_HAVV_VVH_npt[2,ST_HAVV_state],2)
	ST_HAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_HAVV_VVH_npt[1,ST_HAVV_state], ST_HAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_HAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_HAVV_VVM_npt[2,ST_HAVV_state],2)
	ST_HAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_HAVV_VVM_npt[1,ST_HAVV_state], ST_HAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_HAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_HAVV_VVL_npt[2,ST_HAVV_state],2)
	ST_HAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_HAVV_VVL_npt[1,ST_HAVV_state], ST_HAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis V&V - Test phase
	ST_SAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SAVV_VVH_npt[2,ST_SAVV_state],2)
	ST_SAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SAVV_VVH_npt[1,ST_SAVV_state], ST_SAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SAVV_VVM_npt[2,ST_SAVV_state],2)
	ST_SAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SAVV_VVM_npt[1,ST_SAVV_state], ST_SAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_SAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SAVV_VVL_npt[2,ST_SAVV_state],2)
	ST_SAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SAVV_VVL_npt[1,ST_SAVV_state], ST_SAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis V&V - Test phase
	ST_RAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RAVV_VVH_npt[2,ST_RAVV_state],2)
	ST_RAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_RAVV_VVH_npt[1,ST_RAVV_state], ST_RAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_RAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RAVV_VVM_npt[2,ST_RAVV_state],2)
	ST_RAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_RAVV_VVM_npt[1,ST_RAVV_state], ST_RAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_RAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RAVV_VVL_npt[2,ST_RAVV_state],2)
	ST_RAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_RAVV_VVL_npt[1,ST_RAVV_state], ST_RAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Configuration Management V&V - Test phase
	ST_CMVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_CMVV_VVH_npt[2,ST_CMVV_state],2)
	ST_CMVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_CMVV_VVH_npt[1,ST_CMVV_state], ST_CMVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_CMVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_CMVV_VVM_npt[2,ST_CMVV_state],2)
	ST_CMVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_CMVV_VVM_npt[1,ST_CMVV_state], ST_CMVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_CMVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_CMVV_VVL_npt[2,ST_CMVV_state],2)
	ST_CMVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_CMVV_VVL_npt[1,ST_CMVV_state], ST_CMVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Review and Audit V&V - Test phase
	ST_RaAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaAVV_VVH_npt[2,ST_RaAVV_state],2)
	ST_RaAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_RaAVV_VVH_npt[1,ST_RaAVV_state], ST_RaAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_RaAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaAVV_VVM_npt[2,ST_RaAVV_state],2)
	ST_RaAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_RaAVV_VVM_npt[1,ST_RaAVV_state], ST_RaAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_RaAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaAVV_VVL_npt[2,ST_RaAVV_state],2)
	ST_RaAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_RaAVV_VVL_npt[1,ST_RaAVV_state], ST_RaAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Test phase Activity Summary Report Generation
	ST_VVASRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVASRG_VVH_npt[2,ST_VVASRG_state],2)
	ST_VVASRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVASRG_VVH_npt[1,ST_VVASRG_state], ST_VVASRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVASRG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVASRG_VVM_npt[2,ST_VVASRG_state],2)
	ST_VVASRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVASRG_VVM_npt[1,ST_VVASRG_state], ST_VVASRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	ST_VVASRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVASRG_VVL_npt[2,ST_VVASRG_state],2)
	ST_VVASRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVASRG_VVL_npt[1,ST_VVASRG_state], ST_VVASRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(VV=H)P(attribute states|VV=H)
	# m2 = P(VV=M)P(attribute states|VV=M)
	# m3 = P(VV=L)P(attribute states|VV=L)

	ST_VV_m1 <- ST_VVH_prior * ST_VVSITE_VVH_like * ST_VVSQTE_VVH_like * ST_VVSAPG_VVH_like * ST_VVSATE_VVH_like * ST_TAVV_VVH_like * ST_HAVV_VVH_like * ST_SAVV_VVH_like * ST_RAVV_VVH_like * ST_CMVV_VVH_like * ST_RaAVV_VVH_like * ST_VVASRG_VVH_like
	ST_VV_m2 <- ST_VVM_prior * ST_VVSITE_VVM_like * ST_VVSQTE_VVM_like * ST_VVSAPG_VVM_like * ST_VVSATE_VVM_like * ST_TAVV_VVM_like * ST_HAVV_VVM_like * ST_SAVV_VVM_like * ST_RAVV_VVM_like * ST_CMVV_VVM_like * ST_RaAVV_VVM_like * ST_VVASRG_VVM_like
	ST_VV_m3 <- ST_VVL_prior * ST_VVSITE_VVL_like * ST_VVSQTE_VVL_like * ST_VVSAPG_VVL_like * ST_VVSATE_VVL_like * ST_TAVV_VVL_like * ST_HAVV_VVL_like * ST_SAVV_VVL_like * ST_RAVV_VVL_like * ST_CMVV_VVL_like * ST_RaAVV_VVL_like * ST_VVASRG_VVL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	ST_VV_k <- 1 / (ST_VV_m1 + ST_VV_m2 + ST_VV_m3)

	# posterior probability of V&V quality in ST phase
	ST_VVH_post <- ST_VV_k * ST_VV_m1
	ST_VVM_post <- ST_VV_k * ST_VV_m2
	ST_VVL_post <- ST_VV_k * ST_VV_m3


	# Submodel - Test phase

	ST_Defect_passed_from_IM <- IM_Total_Remained_Defect

	# Defect Density likelihood: P(Defect Density|state of Dev quality)
	ST_DevH_DD_like ~ dgamma(1.2439,4.3055)
	ST_DevM_DD_like ~ dgamma(1.5775,3.9236)
	ST_DevL_DD_like ~ dgamma(1.5630,3.1705)

	# Defect density: the integral of P(Dev)*P(Defect Density|Dev) dDev
	ST_Defect_Density <- (ST_DevH_post * ST_DevH_DD_like + ST_DevM_post * ST_DevM_DD_like + ST_DevL_post * ST_DevL_DD_like)

	ST_Defect_introduced_in_current <- ST_FP * ST_Defect_Density

	# Complexity: (FP >= 1000)? High: (FP >= 100)? Medium: Low
	ST_Complexity <- step(ST_FP-1000)+(1-step(ST_FP-1000))*step(ST_FP-100)*2+step(99-ST_FP)*3

	# Defect Detection Probability (current) likelihood: P(DDP_current|state of Dev quality, state of VV quality)
	ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,ST_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (current): the integral of P(DDP_current|Dev, VV) dDev,VV
	ST_Defect_Detection_Probability_current <- ST_DevH_post * ST_VVH_post * ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_current_like + ST_DevH_post * ST_VVM_post * ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_current_like + ST_DevH_post * ST_VVL_post * ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_current_like + ST_DevM_post * ST_VVH_post * ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_current_like + ST_DevM_post * ST_VVM_post * ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_current_like + ST_DevM_post * ST_VVL_post * ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_current_like + ST_DevL_post * ST_VVH_post * ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_current_like + ST_DevL_post * ST_VVM_post * ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_current_like + ST_DevL_post * ST_VVL_post * ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_current_like

	ST_Detected_Defect_current <- ST_Defect_introduced_in_current * ST_Defect_Detection_Probability_current

	ST_Remaining_Defect_current <- ST_Defect_introduced_in_current - ST_Detected_Defect_current

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous) likelihood: P(DDP_previous|state of Dev quality, state of VV quality)
	ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,ST_Complexity])
	ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,ST_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous): the integral of P(DDP_previous|Dev, VV) dDev,VV
	ST_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous <- ST_DevH_post * ST_VVH_post * ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_previous_like + ST_DevH_post * ST_VVM_post * ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_previous_like + ST_DevH_post * ST_VVL_post * ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_previous_like + ST_DevM_post * ST_VVH_post * ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_previous_like + ST_DevM_post * ST_VVM_post * ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_previous_like + ST_DevM_post * ST_VVL_post * ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_previous_like + ST_DevL_post * ST_VVH_post * ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_previous_like + ST_DevL_post * ST_VVM_post * ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_previous_like + ST_DevL_post * ST_VVL_post * ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_previous_like

	ST_Detected_Defect_previous <- ST_Defect_passed_from_IM * ST_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous

	ST_Remaining_Defect_previous <- ST_Defect_passed_from_IM - ST_Detected_Defect_previous

	ST_Total_Remained_Defect <- ST_Remaining_Defect_current + ST_Remaining_Defect_previous


	# Dev Attribute model - Installation & Checkout phase

	# prior probability of Dev quality in IC phase
	IC_DevH_prior ~ dbeta(0.99, 1.66)
	IC_DevM_prior ~ dbeta(1.28, 1.05)
	IC_DevL_prior ~ dbeta(2.83, 32.73)

	# Attribute Installation Procedure Generation

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	IC_IPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IPG_DevH_npt[2,IC_IPG_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of Dev quality)
	IC_IPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_IPG_DevH_npt[1,IC_IPG_state], IC_IPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_IPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IPG_DevM_npt[2,IC_IPG_state],2)
	IC_IPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_IPG_DevM_npt[1,IC_IPG_state], IC_IPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_IPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IPG_DevL_npt[2,IC_IPG_state],2)
	IC_IPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_IPG_DevL_npt[1,IC_IPG_state], IC_IPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Installation and Checkout
	IC_IaC_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IaC_DevH_npt[2,IC_IaC_state],2)
	IC_IaC_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_IaC_DevH_npt[1,IC_IaC_state], IC_IaC_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_IaC_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IaC_DevM_npt[2,IC_IaC_state],2)
	IC_IaC_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_IaC_DevM_npt[1,IC_IaC_state], IC_IaC_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_IaC_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IaC_DevL_npt[2,IC_IaC_state],2)
	IC_IaC_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_IaC_DevL_npt[1,IC_IaC_state], IC_IaC_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis - IC phase
	IC_HA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HA_DevH_npt[2,IC_HA_state],2)
	IC_HA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_HA_DevH_npt[1,IC_HA_state], IC_HA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_HA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HA_DevM_npt[2,IC_HA_state],2)
	IC_HA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_HA_DevM_npt[1,IC_HA_state], IC_HA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_HA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HA_DevL_npt[2,IC_HA_state],2)
	IC_HA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_HA_DevL_npt[1,IC_HA_state], IC_HA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis - IC phase
	IC_SA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SA_DevH_npt[2,IC_SA_state],2)
	IC_SA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_SA_DevH_npt[1,IC_SA_state], IC_SA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_SA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SA_DevM_npt[2,IC_SA_state],2)
	IC_SA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_SA_DevM_npt[1,IC_SA_state], IC_SA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_SA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SA_DevL_npt[2,IC_SA_state],2)
	IC_SA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_SA_DevL_npt[1,IC_SA_state], IC_SA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis - IC phase
	IC_RA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RA_DevH_npt[2,IC_RA_state],2)
	IC_RA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_RA_DevH_npt[1,IC_RA_state], IC_RA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_RA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RA_DevM_npt[2,IC_RA_state],2)
	IC_RA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_RA_DevM_npt[1,IC_RA_state], IC_RA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_RA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RA_DevL_npt[2,IC_RA_state],2)
	IC_RA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_RA_DevL_npt[1,IC_RA_state], IC_RA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(Dev=H)P(attribute states|Dev=H)
	# m2 = P(Dev=M)P(attribute states|Dev=M)
	# m3 = P(Dev=L)P(attribute states|Dev=L)

	IC_Dev_m1 <- IC_DevH_prior * IC_IPG_DevH_like * IC_IaC_DevH_like * IC_HA_DevH_like * IC_SA_DevH_like * IC_RA_DevH_like
	IC_Dev_m2 <- IC_DevM_prior * IC_IPG_DevM_like * IC_IaC_DevM_like * IC_HA_DevM_like * IC_SA_DevM_like * IC_RA_DevM_like
	IC_Dev_m3 <- IC_DevL_prior * IC_IPG_DevL_like * IC_IaC_DevL_like * IC_HA_DevL_like * IC_SA_DevL_like * IC_RA_DevL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	IC_Dev_k <- 1 / (IC_Dev_m1 + IC_Dev_m2 + IC_Dev_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in IC phase
	IC_DevH_post <- IC_Dev_k * IC_Dev_m1
	IC_DevM_post <- IC_Dev_k * IC_Dev_m2
	IC_DevL_post <- IC_Dev_k * IC_Dev_m3


	# V&V Attribute model - Installation & Checkout phase

	# prior probability of V&V quality in IC phase
	IC_VVH_prior ~ dbeta(1.05, 2.26)
	IC_VVM_prior ~ dbeta(1.45, 1.10)
	IC_VVL_prior ~ dbeta(1.28, 8.56)

	# Attribute Installation Configuration Audit V&V

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	IC_ICAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICAVV_VVH_npt[2,IC_ICAVV_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of V&V quality)
	IC_ICAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICAVV_VVH_npt[1,IC_ICAVV_state], IC_ICAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_ICAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICAVV_VVM_npt[2,IC_ICAVV_state],2)
	IC_ICAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICAVV_VVM_npt[1,IC_ICAVV_state], IC_ICAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_ICAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICAVV_VVL_npt[2,IC_ICAVV_state],2)
	IC_ICAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICAVV_VVL_npt[1,IC_ICAVV_state], IC_ICAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Installation Checkout V&V
	IC_ICVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICVV_VVH_npt[2,IC_ICVV_state],2)
	IC_ICVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICVV_VVH_npt[1,IC_ICVV_state], IC_ICVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_ICVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICVV_VVM_npt[2,IC_ICVV_state],2)
	IC_ICVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICVV_VVM_npt[1,IC_ICVV_state], IC_ICVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_ICVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICVV_VVL_npt[2,IC_ICVV_state],2)
	IC_ICVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICVV_VVL_npt[1,IC_ICVV_state], IC_ICVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis V&V
	IC_HAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HAVV_VVH_npt[2,IC_HAVV_state],2)
	IC_HAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_HAVV_VVH_npt[1,IC_HAVV_state], IC_HAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_HAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HAVV_VVM_npt[2,IC_HAVV_state],2)
	IC_HAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_HAVV_VVM_npt[1,IC_HAVV_state], IC_HAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_HAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HAVV_VVL_npt[2,IC_HAVV_state],2)
	IC_HAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_HAVV_VVL_npt[1,IC_HAVV_state], IC_HAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis V&V
	IC_SAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SAVV_VVH_npt[2,IC_SAVV_state],2)
	IC_SAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_SAVV_VVH_npt[1,IC_SAVV_state], IC_SAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_SAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SAVV_VVM_npt[2,IC_SAVV_state],2)
	IC_SAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_SAVV_VVM_npt[1,IC_SAVV_state], IC_SAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_SAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SAVV_VVL_npt[2,IC_SAVV_state],2)
	IC_SAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_SAVV_VVL_npt[1,IC_SAVV_state], IC_SAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis V&V
	IC_RAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RAVV_VVH_npt[2,IC_RAVV_state],2)
	IC_RAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_RAVV_VVH_npt[1,IC_RAVV_state], IC_RAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_RAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RAVV_VVM_npt[2,IC_RAVV_state],2)
	IC_RAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_RAVV_VVM_npt[1,IC_RAVV_state], IC_RAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_RAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RAVV_VVL_npt[2,IC_RAVV_state],2)
	IC_RAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_RAVV_VVL_npt[1,IC_RAVV_state], IC_RAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Installation and Checkout Phase Activity Summary Report Generation
	IC_VVASRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVASRG_VVH_npt[2,IC_VVASRG_state],2)
	IC_VVASRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVASRG_VVH_npt[1,IC_VVASRG_state], IC_VVASRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_VVASRG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVASRG_VVM_npt[2,IC_VVASRG_state],2)
	IC_VVASRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVASRG_VVM_npt[1,IC_VVASRG_state], IC_VVASRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_VVASRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVASRG_VVL_npt[2,IC_VVASRG_state],2)
	IC_VVASRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVASRG_VVL_npt[1,IC_VVASRG_state], IC_VVASRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Final Report Generation
	IC_VVFRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVFRG_VVH_npt[2,IC_VVFRG_state],2)
	IC_VVFRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVFRG_VVH_npt[1,IC_VVFRG_state], IC_VVFRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_VVFRG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVFRG_VVM_npt[2,IC_VVFRG_state],2)
	IC_VVFRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVFRG_VVM_npt[1,IC_VVFRG_state], IC_VVFRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	IC_VVFRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVFRG_VVL_npt[2,IC_VVFRG_state],2)
	IC_VVFRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVFRG_VVL_npt[1,IC_VVFRG_state], IC_VVFRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(VV=H)P(attribute states|VV=H)
	# m2 = P(VV=M)P(attribute states|VV=M)
	# m3 = P(VV=L)P(attribute states|VV=L)

	IC_VV_m1 <- IC_VVH_prior * IC_ICAVV_VVH_like * IC_ICVV_VVH_like * IC_HAVV_VVH_like * IC_SAVV_VVH_like * IC_RAVV_VVH_like * IC_VVASRG_VVH_like * IC_VVFRG_VVH_like
	IC_VV_m2 <- IC_VVM_prior * IC_ICAVV_VVM_like * IC_ICVV_VVM_like * IC_HAVV_VVM_like * IC_SAVV_VVM_like * IC_RAVV_VVM_like * IC_VVASRG_VVM_like * IC_VVFRG_VVM_like
	IC_VV_m3 <- IC_VVL_prior * IC_ICAVV_VVL_like * IC_ICVV_VVL_like * IC_HAVV_VVL_like * IC_SAVV_VVL_like * IC_RAVV_VVL_like * IC_VVASRG_VVL_like * IC_VVFRG_VVL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	IC_VV_k <- 1 / (IC_VV_m1 + IC_VV_m2 + IC_VV_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in IC phase
	IC_VVH_post <- IC_VV_k * IC_VV_m1
	IC_VVM_post <- IC_VV_k * IC_VV_m2
	IC_VVL_post <- IC_VV_k * IC_VV_m3


	# Submodel - Installation & Checkout phase

	IC_Defect_passed_from_ST <- ST_Total_Remained_Defect

	# Defect Density likelihood: P(Defect Density|state of Dev quality)
	IC_DevH_DD_like ~ dgamma(0.6106,3.4640)
	IC_DevM_DD_like ~ dgamma(0.6838,2.6797)
	IC_DevL_DD_like ~ dgamma(0.6514,2.3803)

	# Defect density: the integral of P(Dev)*P(Defect Density|Dev) dDev
	IC_Defect_Density <- (IC_DevH_post * IC_DevH_DD_like + IC_DevM_post * IC_DevM_DD_like + IC_DevL_post * IC_DevL_DD_like)

	IC_Defect_introduced_in_current <- IC_FP * IC_Defect_Density

	# Complexity: (FP >= 1000)? High: (FP >= 100)? Medium: Low
	IC_Complexity <- step(IC_FP-1000)+(1-step(IC_FP-1000))*step(IC_FP-100)*2+step(99-IC_FP)*3

	# Defect Detection Probability (current) likelihood: P(DDP_current|state of VV quality)
	IC_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,IC_Complexity],IC_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,IC_Complexity])
	IC_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,IC_Complexity],IC_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,IC_Complexity])
	IC_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,IC_Complexity],IC_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,IC_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (current): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	IC_Defect_Detection_Probability_current <- IC_VVH_post * IC_VVH_DDP_current_like + IC_VVM_post * IC_VVM_DDP_current_like + IC_VVL_post * IC_VVL_DDP_current_like

	IC_Detected_Defect_current <- IC_Defect_introduced_in_current * IC_Defect_Detection_Probability_current

	IC_Remaining_Defect_current <- IC_Defect_introduced_in_current - IC_Detected_Defect_current

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous) likelihood: P(DDP_previous|state of VV quality)
	IC_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,IC_Complexity],IC_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,IC_Complexity])
	IC_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,IC_Complexity],IC_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,IC_Complexity])
	IC_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,IC_Complexity],IC_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,IC_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	IC_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous <- IC_VVH_post * IC_VVH_DDP_previous_like + IC_VVM_post * IC_VVM_DDP_previous_like + IC_VVL_post * IC_VVL_DDP_previous_like

	IC_Detected_Defect_previous <- IC_Defect_passed_from_ST * IC_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous

	IC_Remaining_Defect_previous <- IC_Defect_passed_from_ST - IC_Detected_Defect_previous

	IC_Total_Remained_Defect <- IC_Remaining_Defect_current + IC_Remaining_Defect_previous




	#### Generic FSD estimation ####
	# Generic Dev Attribute model - Requirement phase

	# Attribute Software Development Planning

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_SR_SDP_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SDP_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_SDP_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of Dev quality)
	generic_SR_SDP_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_SDP_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_SDP_state], generic_SR_SDP_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SDP_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SDP_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_SDP_state],2)
	generic_SR_SDP_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_SDP_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_SDP_state], generic_SR_SDP_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SDP_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SDP_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_SDP_state],2)
	generic_SR_SDP_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_SDP_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_SDP_state], generic_SR_SDP_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Document of a Concept Documentation
	generic_SR_CD_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CD_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_CD_state],2)
	generic_SR_CD_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_CD_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_CD_state], generic_SR_CD_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CD_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CD_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_CD_state],2)
	generic_SR_CD_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_CD_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_CD_state], generic_SR_CD_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CD_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CD_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_CD_state],2)
	generic_SR_CD_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_CD_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_CD_state], generic_SR_CD_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Document of Software Requirements Specifications
	generic_SR_SRS_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SRS_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_SRS_state],2)
	generic_SR_SRS_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_SRS_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_SRS_state], generic_SR_SRS_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SRS_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SRS_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_SRS_state],2)
	generic_SR_SRS_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_SRS_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_SRS_state], generic_SR_SRS_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SRS_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SRS_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_SRS_state],2)
	generic_SR_SRS_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_SRS_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_SRS_state], generic_SR_SRS_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Traceability Analysis
	generic_SR_TA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_TA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_TA_state],2)
	generic_SR_TA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_TA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_TA_state], generic_SR_TA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_TA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_TA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_TA_state],2)
	generic_SR_TA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_TA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_TA_state], generic_SR_TA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_TA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_TA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_TA_state],2)
	generic_SR_TA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_TA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_TA_state], generic_SR_TA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Criticality Analysis
	generic_SR_CA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_CA_state],2)
	generic_SR_CA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_CA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_CA_state], generic_SR_CA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_CA_state],2)
	generic_SR_CA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_CA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_CA_state], generic_SR_CA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_CA_state],2)
	generic_SR_CA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_CA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_CA_state], generic_SR_CA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis
	generic_SR_HA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_HA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_HA_state],2)
	generic_SR_HA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_HA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_HA_state], generic_SR_HA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_HA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_HA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_HA_state],2)
	generic_SR_HA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_HA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_HA_state], generic_SR_HA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_HA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_HA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_HA_state],2)
	generic_SR_HA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_HA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_HA_state], generic_SR_HA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis
	generic_SR_SA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_SA_state],2)
	generic_SR_SA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_SA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_SA_state], generic_SR_SA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_SA_state],2)
	generic_SR_SA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_SA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_SA_state], generic_SR_SA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_SA_state],2)
	generic_SR_SA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_SA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_SA_state], generic_SR_SA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis
	generic_SR_RA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_RA_state],2)
	generic_SR_RA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_RA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_RA_state], generic_SR_RA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_RA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_RA_state],2)
	generic_SR_RA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_RA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_RA_state], generic_SR_RA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_RA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_RA_state],2)
	generic_SR_RA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_RA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_RA_state], generic_SR_RA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute System/Software Qualification Test Plan Generation
	generic_SR_SQTPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SQTPG_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_SQTPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_SQTPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_SQTPG_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_SQTPG_state], generic_SR_SQTPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SQTPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SQTPG_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_SQTPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_SQTPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_SQTPG_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_SQTPG_state], generic_SR_SQTPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SQTPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SQTPG_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_SQTPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_SQTPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_SQTPG_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_SQTPG_state], generic_SR_SQTPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute System/Software Acceptance Test Plan Generation
	generic_SR_SATPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SATPG_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_SATPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_SATPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_SATPG_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_SATPG_state], generic_SR_SATPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SATPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SATPG_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_SATPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_SATPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_SATPG_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_SATPG_state], generic_SR_SATPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SATPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SATPG_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_SATPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_SATPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_SATPG_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_SATPG_state], generic_SR_SATPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Configuration Management
	generic_SR_CM_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CM_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_CM_state],2)
	generic_SR_CM_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_CM_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_CM_state], generic_SR_CM_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CM_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CM_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_CM_state],2)
	generic_SR_CM_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_CM_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_CM_state], generic_SR_CM_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CM_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CM_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_CM_state],2)
	generic_SR_CM_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_CM_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_CM_state], generic_SR_CM_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Review and Audit
	generic_SR_RaA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RaA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SR_RaA_state],2)
	generic_SR_RaA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SR_RaA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SR_RaA_state], generic_SR_RaA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_RaA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RaA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SR_RaA_state],2)
	generic_SR_RaA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SR_RaA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SR_RaA_state], generic_SR_RaA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_RaA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RaA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SR_RaA_state],2)
	generic_SR_RaA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SR_RaA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SR_RaA_state], generic_SR_RaA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(Dev=H)P(attribute states|Dev=H)
	# m2 = P(Dev=M)P(attribute states|Dev=M)
	# m3 = P(Dev=L)P(attribute states|Dev=L)

	generic_SR_Dev_m1 <- SR_DevH_prior * generic_SR_SDP_DevH_like * generic_SR_CD_DevH_like * generic_SR_SRS_DevH_like * generic_SR_TA_DevH_like * generic_SR_CA_DevH_like * generic_SR_HA_DevH_like * generic_SR_SA_DevH_like * generic_SR_RA_DevH_like * generic_SR_SATPG_DevH_like * generic_SR_CM_DevH_like * generic_SR_RaA_DevH_like
	generic_SR_Dev_m2 <- SR_DevM_prior * generic_SR_SDP_DevM_like * generic_SR_CD_DevM_like * generic_SR_SRS_DevM_like * generic_SR_TA_DevM_like * generic_SR_CA_DevM_like * generic_SR_HA_DevM_like * generic_SR_SA_DevM_like * generic_SR_RA_DevM_like * generic_SR_SATPG_DevM_like * generic_SR_CM_DevM_like * generic_SR_RaA_DevM_like
	generic_SR_Dev_m3 <- SR_DevL_prior * generic_SR_SDP_DevL_like * generic_SR_CD_DevL_like * generic_SR_SRS_DevL_like * generic_SR_TA_DevL_like * generic_SR_CA_DevL_like * generic_SR_HA_DevL_like * generic_SR_SA_DevL_like * generic_SR_RA_DevL_like * generic_SR_SATPG_DevL_like * generic_SR_CM_DevL_like * generic_SR_RaA_DevL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_SR_Dev_k <- 1 / (generic_SR_Dev_m1 + generic_SR_Dev_m2 + generic_SR_Dev_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in SR phase
	generic_SR_DevH_post <- generic_SR_Dev_k * generic_SR_Dev_m1
	generic_SR_DevM_post <- generic_SR_Dev_k * generic_SR_Dev_m2
	generic_SR_DevL_post <- generic_SR_Dev_k * generic_SR_Dev_m3


	# Generic V&V Attribute model - Requirement phase

	# Attribute Software V&V Planning

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_SR_SVVP_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SVVP_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_SVVP_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of V&V quality)
	generic_SR_SVVP_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_SVVP_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_SVVP_state], generic_SR_SVVP_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SVVP_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SVVP_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_SVVP_state],2)
	generic_SR_SVVP_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_SVVP_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_SVVP_state], generic_SR_SVVP_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SVVP_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SVVP_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_SVVP_state],2)
	generic_SR_SVVP_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_SVVP_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_SVVP_state], generic_SR_SVVP_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Concept Documentation Evaluation
	generic_SR_CDE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CDE_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_CDE_state],2)
	generic_SR_CDE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_CDE_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_CDE_state], generic_SR_CDE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CDE_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CDE_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_CDE_state],2)
	generic_SR_CDE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_CDE_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_CDE_state], generic_SR_CDE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CDE_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CDE_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_CDE_state],2)
	generic_SR_CDE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_CDE_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_CDE_state], generic_SR_CDE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hardware/Software/User Requirements Allocation Analysis
	generic_SR_HRAA_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_HRAA_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_HRAA_state],2)
	generic_SR_HRAA_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_HRAA_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_HRAA_state], generic_SR_HRAA_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_HRAA_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_HRAA_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_HRAA_state],2)
	generic_SR_HRAA_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_HRAA_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_HRAA_state], generic_SR_HRAA_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_HRAA_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_HRAA_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_HRAA_state], generic_SR_HRAA_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Document of Software Requirements Evaluation
	generic_SR_SRE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SRE_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_SRE_state],2)
	generic_SR_SRE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_SRE_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_SRE_state], generic_SR_SRE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SRE_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SRE_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_SRE_state],2)
	generic_SR_SRE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_SRE_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_SRE_state], generic_SR_SRE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SRE_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SRE_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_SRE_state],2)
	generic_SR_SRE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_SRE_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_SRE_state], generic_SR_SRE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Interface Analysis V&V
	generic_SR_IAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_IAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_IAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_IAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_IAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_IAVV_state], generic_SR_IAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_IAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_IAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_IAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_IAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_IAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_IAVV_state], generic_SR_IAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_IAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_IAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_IAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_IAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_IAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_IAVV_state], generic_SR_IAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Traceability Analysis V&V
	generic_SR_TAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_TAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_TAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_TAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_TAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_TAVV_state], generic_SR_TAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_TAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_TAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_TAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_TAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_TAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_TAVV_state], generic_SR_TAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_TAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_TAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_TAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_TAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_TAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_TAVV_state], generic_SR_TAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Criticality Analysis V&V
	generic_SR_CAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_CAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_CAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_CAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_CAVV_state], generic_SR_CAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_CAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_CAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_CAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_CAVV_state], generic_SR_CAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_CAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_CAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_CAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_CAVV_state], generic_SR_CAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis V&V
	generic_SR_HAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_HAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_HAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_HAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_HAVV_state], generic_SR_HAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_HAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_HAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_HAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_HAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_HAVV_state], generic_SR_HAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_HAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_HAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_HAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_HAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_HAVV_state], generic_SR_HAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis V&V
	generic_SR_SAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_SAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_SAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_SAVV_state], generic_SR_SAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_SAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_SAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_SAVV_state], generic_SR_SAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_SAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_SAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_SAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_SAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_SAVV_state], generic_SR_SAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis V&V
	generic_SR_RAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_RAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_RAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_RAVV_state], generic_SR_RAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_RAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_RAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_RAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_RAVV_state], generic_SR_RAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_RAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_RAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_RAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_RAVV_state], generic_SR_RAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V System/Software Quantification Test Plan Generation
	generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_VVSQTPG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_VVSQTPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_VVSQTPG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_VVSQTPG_state], generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_VVSQTPG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_VVSQTPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_VVSQTPG_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_VVSQTPG_state], generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_VVSQTPG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_VVSQTPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_VVSQTPG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_VVSQTPG_state], generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Acceptance Test Plan Generation
	generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_VVSATPG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_VVSATPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_VVSATPG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_VVSATPG_state], generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_VVSATPG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_VVSATPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_VVSATPG_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_VVSATPG_state], generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_VVSATPG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_VVSATPG_state],2)
	generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_VVSATPG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_VVSATPG_state], generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Configuration Management Assessment
	generic_SR_CMA_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CMA_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_CMA_state],2)
	generic_SR_CMA_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_CMA_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_CMA_state], generic_SR_CMA_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CMA_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CMA_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_CMA_state],2)
	generic_SR_CMA_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_CMA_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_CMA_state], generic_SR_CMA_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_CMA_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_CMA_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_CMA_state],2)
	generic_SR_CMA_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_CMA_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_CMA_state], generic_SR_CMA_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Reviews and Audit V&V
	generic_SR_RaAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RaAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_RaAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_RaAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_RaAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_RaAVV_state], generic_SR_RaAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_RaAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RaAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_RaAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_RaAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_RaAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_RaAVV_state], generic_SR_RaAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_RaAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_RaAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_RaAVV_state],2)
	generic_SR_RaAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_RaAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_RaAVV_state], generic_SR_RaAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Requirements Specifications Phase Activity Summary Report Generation
	generic_SR_VVASRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_VVASRG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SR_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_SR_VVASRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SR_VVASRG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SR_VVASRG_state], generic_SR_VVASRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_VVASRG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_VVASRG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SR_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_SR_VVASRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SR_VVASRG_VVM_npt[1,generic_SR_VVASRG_state], generic_SR_VVASRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SR_VVASRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SR_VVASRG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SR_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_SR_VVASRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SR_VVASRG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SR_VVASRG_state], generic_SR_VVASRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(VV=H)P(attribute states|VV=H)
	# m2 = P(VV=M)P(attribute states|VV=M)
	# m3 = P(VV=L)P(attribute states|VV=L)

	generic_SR_VV_m1 <- SR_VVH_prior * generic_SR_SVVP_VVH_like * generic_SR_CDE_VVH_like * generic_SR_HRAA_VVH_like * generic_SR_SRE_VVH_like * generic_SR_IAVV_VVH_like * generic_SR_TAVV_VVH_like * generic_SR_CAVV_VVH_like * generic_SR_HAVV_VVH_like * generic_SR_SAVV_VVH_like * generic_SR_RAVV_VVH_like * generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVH_like * generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVH_like * generic_SR_CMA_VVH_like * generic_SR_RaAVV_VVH_like * generic_SR_VVASRG_VVH_like
	generic_SR_VV_m2 <- SR_VVM_prior * generic_SR_SVVP_VVM_like * generic_SR_CDE_VVM_like * generic_SR_HRAA_VVM_like * generic_SR_SRE_VVM_like * generic_SR_IAVV_VVM_like * generic_SR_TAVV_VVM_like * generic_SR_CAVV_VVM_like * generic_SR_HAVV_VVM_like * generic_SR_SAVV_VVM_like * generic_SR_RAVV_VVM_like * generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVM_like * generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVM_like * generic_SR_CMA_VVM_like * generic_SR_RaAVV_VVM_like * generic_SR_VVASRG_VVM_like
	generic_SR_VV_m3 <- SR_VVL_prior * generic_SR_SVVP_VVL_like * generic_SR_CDE_VVL_like * generic_SR_HRAA_VVL_like * generic_SR_SRE_VVL_like * generic_SR_IAVV_VVL_like * generic_SR_TAVV_VVL_like * generic_SR_CAVV_VVL_like * generic_SR_HAVV_VVL_like * generic_SR_SAVV_VVL_like * generic_SR_RAVV_VVL_like * generic_SR_VVSQTPG_VVL_like * generic_SR_VVSATPG_VVL_like * generic_SR_CMA_VVL_like * generic_SR_RaAVV_VVL_like * generic_SR_VVASRG_VVL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_SR_VV_k <- 1 / (generic_SR_VV_m1 + generic_SR_VV_m2 + generic_SR_VV_m3)

	# posterior probability of V&V quality in SR phase
	generic_SR_VVH_post <- generic_SR_VV_k * generic_SR_VV_m1
	generic_SR_VVM_post <- generic_SR_VV_k * generic_SR_VV_m2
	generic_SR_VVL_post <- generic_SR_VV_k * generic_SR_VV_m3


	# Generic Submodel - Requirement phase

	# Defect density: the integral of P(Dev)*P(Defect Density|Dev) dDev
	generic_SR_Defect_Density <- (generic_SR_DevH_post * SR_DevH_DD_like + generic_SR_DevM_post * SR_DevM_DD_like + generic_SR_DevL_post * SR_DevL_DD_like)

	generic_SR_Defect_introduced_in_current <- generic_SR_FP * generic_SR_Defect_Density

	# Complexity: (FP >= 1000)? High: (FP >= 100)? Medium: Low
	generic_SR_Complexity <- step(generic_SR_FP-1000)+(1-step(generic_SR_FP-1000))*step(generic_SR_FP-100)*2+step(99-generic_SR_FP)*3

	# Defect Detection Probability (current) likelihood: P(DDP_current|state of VV quality)
	generic_SR_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(SR_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_SR_Complexity],SR_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_SR_Complexity])
	generic_SR_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(SR_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_SR_Complexity],SR_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_SR_Complexity])
	generic_SR_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(SR_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_SR_Complexity],SR_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_SR_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (current): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	generic_SR_Defect_Detection_Probability_current <- (generic_SR_VVH_post * generic_SR_VVH_DDP_current_like + generic_SR_VVM_post * generic_SR_VVM_DDP_current_like + generic_SR_VVL_post * generic_SR_VVL_DDP_current_like)

	generic_SR_Detected_Defect_current <- generic_SR_Defect_introduced_in_current * generic_SR_Defect_Detection_Probability_current

	generic_SR_Remaining_Defect_current <- generic_SR_Defect_introduced_in_current - generic_SR_Detected_Defect_current

	# since there's no phase before the SR phase
	generic_SR_Total_Remained_Defect <- generic_SR_Remaining_Defect_current


	# Generic Dev Attribute model - Design phase

	# Attribute Development of Software Architecture Description

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_SD_SAD_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SAD_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_SAD_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of Dev quality)
	generic_SD_SAD_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SAD_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_SAD_state], generic_SD_SAD_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SAD_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SAD_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_SAD_state],2)
	generic_SD_SAD_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SAD_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_SAD_state], generic_SD_SAD_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SAD_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SAD_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_SAD_state],2)
	generic_SD_SAD_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SAD_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_SAD_state], generic_SD_SAD_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Development of Software Design Description
	generic_SD_SDD_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SDD_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_SDD_state],2)
	generic_SD_SDD_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SDD_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_SDD_state], generic_SD_SDD_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SDD_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SDD_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_SDD_state],2)
	generic_SD_SDD_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SDD_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_SDD_state], generic_SD_SDD_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SDD_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SDD_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_SDD_state],2)
	generic_SD_SDD_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SDD_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_SDD_state], generic_SD_SDD_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Traceability Analysis - Design Phase
	generic_SD_TA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_TA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_TA_state],2)
	generic_SD_TA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_TA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_TA_state], generic_SD_TA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_TA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_TA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_TA_state],2)
	generic_SD_TA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_TA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_TA_state], generic_SD_TA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_TA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_TA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_TA_state],2)
	generic_SD_TA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_TA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_TA_state], generic_SD_TA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Criticality Analysis - Design Phase
	generic_SD_CA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_CA_state],2)
	generic_SD_CA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_CA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_CA_state], generic_SD_CA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_CA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_CA_state],2)
	generic_SD_CA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_CA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_CA_state], generic_SD_CA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_CA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_CA_state],2)
	generic_SD_CA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_CA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_CA_state], generic_SD_CA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis - Design Phase
	generic_SD_HA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_HA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_HA_state],2)
	generic_SD_HA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_HA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_HA_state], generic_SD_HA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_HA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_HA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_HA_state],2)
	generic_SD_HA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_HA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_HA_state], generic_SD_HA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_HA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_HA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_HA_state],2)
	generic_SD_HA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_HA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_HA_state], generic_SD_HA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis - Design Phase
	generic_SD_SA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_SA_state],2)
	generic_SD_SA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_SA_state], generic_SD_SA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_SA_state],2)
	generic_SD_SA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_SA_state], generic_SD_SA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_SA_state],2)
	generic_SD_SA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_SA_state], generic_SD_SA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis - Design Phase
	generic_SD_RA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_RA_state],2)
	generic_SD_RA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_RA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_RA_state], generic_SD_RA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_RA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_RA_state],2)
	generic_SD_RA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_RA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_RA_state], generic_SD_RA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_RA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_RA_state],2)
	generic_SD_RA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_RA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_RA_state], generic_SD_RA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Component Test Plan Generation
	generic_SD_SCTPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SCTPG_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_SCTPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SCTPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SCTPG_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_SCTPG_state], generic_SD_SCTPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SCTPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SCTPG_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_SCTPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SCTPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SCTPG_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_SCTPG_state], generic_SD_SCTPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SCTPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SCTPG_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_SCTPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SCTPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SCTPG_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_SCTPG_state], generic_SD_SCTPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Integration Test Plan Generation
	generic_SD_SITPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SITPG_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_SITPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SITPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SITPG_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_SITPG_state], generic_SD_SITPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SITPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SITPG_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_SITPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SITPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SITPG_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_SITPG_state], generic_SD_SITPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SITPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SITPG_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_SITPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SITPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SITPG_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_SITPG_state], generic_SD_SITPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Component Test Design Generation
	generic_SD_SCTDG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SCTDG_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_SCTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SCTDG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SCTDG_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_SCTDG_state], generic_SD_SCTDG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SCTDG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SCTDG_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_SCTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SCTDG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SCTDG_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_SCTDG_state], generic_SD_SCTDG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SCTDG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SCTDG_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_SCTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SCTDG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SCTDG_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_SCTDG_state], generic_SD_SCTDG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Integration Test Design Generation
	generic_SD_SITDG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SITDG_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_SITDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SITDG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SITDG_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_SITDG_state], generic_SD_SITDG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SITDG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SITDG_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_SITDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SITDG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SITDG_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_SITDG_state], generic_SD_SITDG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SITDG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SITDG_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_SITDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SITDG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SITDG_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_SITDG_state], generic_SD_SITDG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Qualification Test Design Generation
	generic_SD_SQTDG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SQTDG_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_SQTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SQTDG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SQTDG_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_SQTDG_state], generic_SD_SQTDG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SQTDG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SQTDG_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_SQTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SQTDG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SQTDG_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_SQTDG_state], generic_SD_SQTDG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SQTDG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SQTDG_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_SQTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SQTDG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SQTDG_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_SQTDG_state], generic_SD_SQTDG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Acceptance Test Design Generation
	generic_SD_SATDG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SATDG_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_SATDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SATDG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SATDG_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_SATDG_state], generic_SD_SATDG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SATDG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SATDG_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_SATDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SATDG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SATDG_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_SATDG_state], generic_SD_SATDG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SATDG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SATDG_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_SATDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_SATDG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SATDG_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_SATDG_state], generic_SD_SATDG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Configuration Management - Design Phase
	generic_SD_CM_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CM_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_CM_state],2)
	generic_SD_CM_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_CM_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_CM_state], generic_SD_CM_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_CM_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CM_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_CM_state],2)
	generic_SD_CM_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_CM_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_CM_state], generic_SD_CM_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_CM_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CM_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_CM_state],2)
	generic_SD_CM_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_CM_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_CM_state], generic_SD_CM_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Reviews and Audit - Design Phase
	generic_SD_RaA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RaA_DevH_npt[2,generic_SD_RaA_state],2)
	generic_SD_RaA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(SD_RaA_DevH_npt[1,generic_SD_RaA_state], generic_SD_RaA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_RaA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RaA_DevM_npt[2,generic_SD_RaA_state],2)
	generic_SD_RaA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(SD_RaA_DevM_npt[1,generic_SD_RaA_state], generic_SD_RaA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_RaA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RaA_DevL_npt[2,generic_SD_RaA_state],2)
	generic_SD_RaA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(SD_RaA_DevL_npt[1,generic_SD_RaA_state], generic_SD_RaA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(Dev=H)P(attribute states|Dev=H)
	# m2 = P(Dev=M)P(attribute states|Dev=M)
	# m3 = P(Dev=L)P(attribute states|Dev=L)

	generic_SD_Dev_m1 <- SD_DevH_prior * generic_SD_SAD_DevH_like * generic_SD_SDD_DevH_like * generic_SD_TA_DevH_like * generic_SD_CA_DevH_like * generic_SD_HA_DevH_like * generic_SD_SA_DevH_like * generic_SD_RA_DevH_like * generic_SD_SCTPG_DevH_like * generic_SD_SITPG_DevH_like * generic_SD_SCTDG_DevH_like * generic_SD_SITDG_DevH_like * generic_SD_SQTDG_DevH_like * generic_SD_SATDG_DevH_like * generic_SD_CM_DevH_like * generic_SD_RaA_DevH_like
	generic_SD_Dev_m2 <- SD_DevM_prior * generic_SD_SAD_DevM_like * generic_SD_SDD_DevM_like * generic_SD_TA_DevM_like * generic_SD_CA_DevM_like * generic_SD_HA_DevM_like * generic_SD_SA_DevM_like * generic_SD_RA_DevM_like * generic_SD_SCTPG_DevM_like * generic_SD_SITPG_DevM_like * generic_SD_SCTDG_DevM_like * generic_SD_SITDG_DevM_like * generic_SD_SQTDG_DevM_like * generic_SD_SATDG_DevM_like * generic_SD_CM_DevM_like * generic_SD_RaA_DevM_like
	generic_SD_Dev_m3 <- SD_DevL_prior * generic_SD_SAD_DevL_like * generic_SD_SDD_DevL_like * generic_SD_TA_DevL_like * generic_SD_CA_DevL_like * generic_SD_HA_DevL_like * generic_SD_SA_DevL_like * generic_SD_RA_DevL_like * generic_SD_SCTPG_DevL_like * generic_SD_SITPG_DevL_like * generic_SD_SCTDG_DevL_like * generic_SD_SITDG_DevL_like * generic_SD_SQTDG_DevL_like * generic_SD_SATDG_DevL_like * generic_SD_CM_DevL_like * generic_SD_RaA_DevL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_SD_Dev_k <- 1 / (generic_SD_Dev_m1 + generic_SD_Dev_m2 + generic_SD_Dev_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in SD phase
	generic_SD_DevH_post <- generic_SD_Dev_k * generic_SD_Dev_m1
	generic_SD_DevM_post <- generic_SD_Dev_k * generic_SD_Dev_m2
	generic_SD_DevL_post <- generic_SD_Dev_k * generic_SD_Dev_m3


	# Generic V&V Attribute model - Design phase

	# Attribute Design Evaluation

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_SD_DE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_DE_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_DE_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of V&V quality)
	generic_SD_DE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_DE_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_DE_state], generic_SD_DE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_DE_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_DE_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_DE_state],2)
	generic_SD_DE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_DE_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_DE_state], generic_SD_DE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_DE_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_DE_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_DE_state],2)
	generic_SD_DE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_DE_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_DE_state], generic_SD_DE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Interface Analysis V&V
	generic_SD_IAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_IAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_IAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_IAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_IAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_IAVV_state], generic_SD_IAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_IAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_IAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_IAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_IAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_IAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_IAVV_state], generic_SD_IAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_IAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_IAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_IAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_IAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_IAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_IAVV_state], generic_SD_IAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Traceability Analysis V&V - Design Phase
	generic_SD_TAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_TAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_TAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_TAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_TAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_TAVV_state], generic_SD_TAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_TAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_TAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_TAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_TAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_TAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_TAVV_state], generic_SD_TAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_TAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_TAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_TAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_TAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_TAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_TAVV_state], generic_SD_TAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Criticality Analysis V&V - Design Phase
	generic_SD_CAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_CAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_CAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_CAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_CAVV_state], generic_SD_CAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_CAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_CAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_CAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_CAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_CAVV_state], generic_SD_CAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_CAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_CAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_CAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_CAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_CAVV_state], generic_SD_CAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis V&V - Design Phase
	generic_SD_HAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_HAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_HAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_HAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_HAVV_state], generic_SD_HAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_HAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_HAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_HAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_HAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_HAVV_state], generic_SD_HAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_HAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_HAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_HAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_HAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_HAVV_state], generic_SD_HAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis V&V - Design Phase
	generic_SD_SAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_SAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_SAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_SAVV_state], generic_SD_SAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_SAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_SAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_SAVV_state], generic_SD_SAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_SAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_SAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_SAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_SAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_SAVV_state], generic_SD_SAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis V&V - Design Phase
	generic_SD_RAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_RAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_RAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_RAVV_state], generic_SD_RAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_RAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_RAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_RAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_RAVV_state], generic_SD_RAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_RAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_RAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_RAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_RAVV_state], generic_SD_RAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Component Test Plan Generation
	generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSCTPG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSCTPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSCTPG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSCTPG_state], generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSCTPG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSCTPG_state],2)
