	generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSCTPG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSCTPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSCTPG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSCTPG_state], generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Integration Test Plan Generation
	generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSITPG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSITPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSITPG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSITPG_state], generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSITPG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSITPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSITPG_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSITPG_state], generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSITPG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSITPG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSITPG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSITPG_state], generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Component Test Design Generation
	generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSCTDG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSCTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSCTDG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSCTDG_state], generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSCTDG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSCTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSCTDG_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSCTDG_state], generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSCTDG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSCTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSCTDG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSCTDG_state], generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Integration Test Design Generation
	generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSITDG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSITDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSITDG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSITDG_state], generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSITDG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSITDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSITDG_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSITDG_state], generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSITDG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSITDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSITDG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSITDG_state], generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Qualification Test Design Generation
	generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSQTDG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSQTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSQTDG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSQTDG_state], generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSQTDG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSQTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSQTDG_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSQTDG_state], generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSQTDG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSQTDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSQTDG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSQTDG_state], generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Acceptance Test Design Generation
	generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSATDG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSATDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSATDG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSATDG_state], generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSATDG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSATDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSATDG_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSATDG_state], generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVSATDG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_VVSATDG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVSATDG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_VVSATDG_state], generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Configuration Management V&V - Design Phase
	generic_SD_CMVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CMVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_CMVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_CMVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_CMVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_CMVV_state], generic_SD_CMVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_CMVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CMVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_CMVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_CMVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_CMVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_CMVV_state], generic_SD_CMVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_CMVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_CMVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_CMVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_CMVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_CMVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_CMVV_state], generic_SD_CMVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Review and Audit V&V - Design Phase
	generic_SD_RaAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RaAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_RaAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_RaAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_RaAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_RaAVV_state], generic_SD_RaAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_RaAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RaAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_RaAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_RaAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_RaAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_RaAVV_state], generic_SD_RaAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_RaAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_RaAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_RaAVV_state],2)
	generic_SD_RaAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_RaAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_RaAVV_state], generic_SD_RaAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Design Phase Activity Summary Report Generation
	generic_SD_VVASRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVASRG_VVH_npt[2,generic_SD_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVASRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVASRG_VVH_npt[1,generic_SD_VVASRG_state], generic_SD_VVASRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVASRG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVASRG_VVM_npt[2,generic_SD_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVASRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVASRG_VVM_npt[1,generic_SD_VVASRG_state], generic_SD_VVASRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_SD_VVASRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(SD_VVASRG_VVL_npt[2,generic_SD_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_SD_VVASRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(SD_VVASRG_VVL_npt[1,generic_SD_VVASRG_state], generic_SD_VVASRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(VV=H)P(attribute states|VV=H)
	# m2 = P(VV=M)P(attribute states|VV=M)
	# m3 = P(VV=L)P(attribute states|VV=L)

	generic_SD_VV_m1 <- SD_VVH_prior * generic_SD_DE_VVH_like * generic_SD_IAVV_VVH_like * generic_SD_TAVV_VVH_like * generic_SD_CAVV_VVH_like * generic_SD_HAVV_VVH_like * generic_SD_SAVV_VVH_like * generic_SD_RAVV_VVH_like * generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVH_like * generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVH_like * generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVH_like * generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVH_like * generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVH_like * generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVH_like * generic_SD_CMVV_VVH_like * generic_SD_RaAVV_VVH_like * generic_SD_VVASRG_VVH_like
	generic_SD_VV_m2 <- SD_VVM_prior * generic_SD_DE_VVM_like * generic_SD_IAVV_VVM_like * generic_SD_TAVV_VVM_like * generic_SD_CAVV_VVM_like * generic_SD_HAVV_VVM_like * generic_SD_SAVV_VVM_like * generic_SD_RAVV_VVM_like * generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVM_like * generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVM_like * generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVM_like * generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVM_like * generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVM_like * generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVM_like * generic_SD_CMVV_VVM_like * generic_SD_RaAVV_VVM_like * generic_SD_VVASRG_VVM_like
	generic_SD_VV_m3 <- SD_VVL_prior * generic_SD_DE_VVL_like * generic_SD_IAVV_VVL_like * generic_SD_TAVV_VVL_like * generic_SD_CAVV_VVL_like * generic_SD_HAVV_VVL_like * generic_SD_SAVV_VVL_like * generic_SD_RAVV_VVL_like * generic_SD_VVSCTPG_VVL_like * generic_SD_VVSITPG_VVL_like * generic_SD_VVSCTDG_VVL_like * generic_SD_VVSITDG_VVL_like * generic_SD_VVSQTDG_VVL_like * generic_SD_VVSATDG_VVL_like * generic_SD_CMVV_VVL_like * generic_SD_RaAVV_VVL_like * generic_SD_VVASRG_VVL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_SD_VV_k <- 1 / (generic_SD_VV_m1 + generic_SD_VV_m2 + generic_SD_VV_m3)

	# posterior probability of V&V quality in SD phase
	generic_SD_VVH_post <- generic_SD_VV_k * generic_SD_VV_m1
	generic_SD_VVM_post <- generic_SD_VV_k * generic_SD_VV_m2
	generic_SD_VVL_post <- generic_SD_VV_k * generic_SD_VV_m3


	# Generic Submodel - Design phase

	generic_SD_Defect_passed_from_SR <- generic_SR_Total_Remained_Defect

	# Defect density: the integral of P(Dev)*P(Defect Density|Dev) dDev
	generic_SD_Defect_Density <- (generic_SD_DevH_post * SD_DevH_DD_like + generic_SD_DevM_post * SD_DevM_DD_like + generic_SD_DevL_post * SD_DevL_DD_like)

	generic_SD_Defect_introduced_in_current <- generic_SD_FP * generic_SD_Defect_Density

	# Complexity: (FP >= 1000)? High: (FP >= 100)? Medium: Low
	generic_SD_Complexity <- step(generic_SD_FP-1000)+(1-step(generic_SD_FP-1000))*step(generic_SD_FP-100)*2+step(99-generic_SD_FP)*3

	# Defect Detection Probability (current) likelihood: P(DDP_current|state of VV quality)
	generic_SD_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(SD_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_SD_Complexity],SD_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_SD_Complexity])
	generic_SD_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(SD_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_SD_Complexity],SD_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_SD_Complexity])
	generic_SD_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(SD_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_SD_Complexity],SD_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_SD_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (current): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	generic_SD_Defect_Detection_Probability_current <- generic_SD_VVH_post * generic_SD_VVH_DDP_current_like + generic_SD_VVM_post * generic_SD_VVM_DDP_current_like + generic_SD_VVL_post * generic_SD_VVL_DDP_current_like

	generic_SD_Detected_Defect_current <- generic_SD_Defect_introduced_in_current * generic_SD_Defect_Detection_Probability_current

	generic_SD_Remaining_Defect_current <- generic_SD_Defect_introduced_in_current - generic_SD_Detected_Defect_current

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous) likelihood: P(DDP_previous|state of VV quality)
	generic_SD_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(SD_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_SD_Complexity],SD_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_SD_Complexity])
	generic_SD_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(SD_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_SD_Complexity],SD_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_SD_Complexity])
	generic_SD_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(SD_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_SD_Complexity],SD_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_SD_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous): the integral of P(DDP_previous|VV) dVV
	generic_SD_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous <- generic_SD_VVH_post * generic_SD_VVH_DDP_previous_like + generic_SD_VVM_post * generic_SD_VVM_DDP_previous_like + generic_SD_VVL_post * generic_SD_VVL_DDP_previous_like

	generic_SD_Detected_Defect_previous <- generic_SD_Defect_passed_from_SR * generic_SD_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous

	generic_SD_Remaining_Defect_previous <- generic_SD_Defect_passed_from_SR - generic_SD_Detected_Defect_previous

	generic_SD_Total_Remained_Defect <- generic_SD_Remaining_Defect_current + generic_SD_Remaining_Defect_previous


	# Generic Dev Attribute model - Implementation phase

	# Attribute Source Code and Source Code Documentation Generation

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCaSCDG_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_SCaSCDG_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of Dev quality)
	generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCaSCDG_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_SCaSCDG_state], generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCaSCDG_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_SCaSCDG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCaSCDG_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_SCaSCDG_state], generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCaSCDG_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_SCaSCDG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCaSCDG_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_SCaSCDG_state], generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Traceability Analysis
	generic_IM_TA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_TA_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_TA_state],2)
	generic_IM_TA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_TA_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_TA_state], generic_IM_TA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_TA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_TA_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_TA_state],2)
	generic_IM_TA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_TA_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_TA_state], generic_IM_TA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_TA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_TA_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_TA_state],2)
	generic_IM_TA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_TA_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_TA_state], generic_IM_TA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Criticality Analysis
	generic_IM_CA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CA_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_CA_state],2)
	generic_IM_CA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_CA_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_CA_state], generic_IM_CA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CA_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_CA_state],2)
	generic_IM_CA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_CA_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_CA_state], generic_IM_CA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CA_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_CA_state],2)
	generic_IM_CA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_CA_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_CA_state], generic_IM_CA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis
	generic_IM_HA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_HA_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_HA_state],2)
	generic_IM_HA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_HA_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_HA_state], generic_IM_HA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_HA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_HA_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_HA_state],2)
	generic_IM_HA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_HA_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_HA_state], generic_IM_HA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_HA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_HA_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_HA_state],2)
	generic_IM_HA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_HA_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_HA_state], generic_IM_HA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis
	generic_IM_SA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SA_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_SA_state],2)
	generic_IM_SA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SA_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_SA_state], generic_IM_SA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SA_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_SA_state],2)
	generic_IM_SA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SA_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_SA_state], generic_IM_SA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SA_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_SA_state],2)
	generic_IM_SA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SA_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_SA_state], generic_IM_SA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis
	generic_IM_RA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RA_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_RA_state],2)
	generic_IM_RA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_RA_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_RA_state], generic_IM_RA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_RA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RA_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_RA_state],2)
	generic_IM_RA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_RA_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_RA_state], generic_IM_RA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_RA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RA_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_RA_state],2)
	generic_IM_RA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_RA_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_RA_state], generic_IM_RA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Component Test Case Generation
	generic_IM_CTCG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CTCG_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_CTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_CTCG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_CTCG_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_CTCG_state], generic_IM_CTCG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CTCG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CTCG_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_CTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_CTCG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_CTCG_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_CTCG_state], generic_IM_CTCG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CTCG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CTCG_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_CTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_CTCG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_CTCG_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_CTCG_state], generic_IM_CTCG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Integration Test Case Generation
	generic_IM_SITCG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SITCG_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_SITCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SITCG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SITCG_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_SITCG_state], generic_IM_SITCG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SITCG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SITCG_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_SITCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SITCG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SITCG_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_SITCG_state], generic_IM_SITCG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SITCG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SITCG_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_SITCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SITCG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SITCG_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_SITCG_state], generic_IM_SITCG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Quantification Test Case Generation
	generic_IM_SQTCG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SQTCG_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_SQTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SQTCG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SQTCG_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_SQTCG_state], generic_IM_SQTCG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SQTCG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SQTCG_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_SQTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SQTCG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SQTCG_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_SQTCG_state], generic_IM_SQTCG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SQTCG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SQTCG_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_SQTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SQTCG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SQTCG_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_SQTCG_state], generic_IM_SQTCG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Acceptance Test Case Generation
	generic_IM_SATCG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SATCG_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_SATCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SATCG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SATCG_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_SATCG_state], generic_IM_SATCG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SATCG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SATCG_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_SATCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SATCG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SATCG_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_SATCG_state], generic_IM_SATCG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SATCG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SATCG_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_SATCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SATCG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SATCG_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_SATCG_state], generic_IM_SATCG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Component Test Procedure Generation
	generic_IM_SCTPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCTPG_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_SCTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCTPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCTPG_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_SCTPG_state], generic_IM_SCTPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SCTPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCTPG_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_SCTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCTPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCTPG_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_SCTPG_state], generic_IM_SCTPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SCTPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCTPG_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_SCTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCTPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCTPG_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_SCTPG_state], generic_IM_SCTPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Integration Test Procedure Generation
	generic_IM_SITPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SITPG_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_SITPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SITPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SITPG_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_SITPG_state], generic_IM_SITPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SITPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SITPG_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_SITPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SITPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SITPG_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_SITPG_state], generic_IM_SITPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SITPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SITPG_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_SITPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SITPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SITPG_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_SITPG_state], generic_IM_SITPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Quantification Test Procedure Generation
	generic_IM_SQTPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SQTPG_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_SQTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SQTPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SQTPG_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_SQTPG_state], generic_IM_SQTPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SQTPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SQTPG_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_SQTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SQTPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SQTPG_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_SQTPG_state], generic_IM_SQTPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SQTPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SQTPG_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_SQTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_SQTPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SQTPG_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_SQTPG_state], generic_IM_SQTPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Configuration Management
	generic_IM_CM_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CM_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_CM_state],2)
	generic_IM_CM_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_CM_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_CM_state], generic_IM_CM_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CM_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CM_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_CM_state],2)
	generic_IM_CM_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_CM_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_CM_state], generic_IM_CM_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CM_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CM_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_CM_state],2)
	generic_IM_CM_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_CM_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_CM_state], generic_IM_CM_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Reviews and Audits
	generic_IM_RaA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RaA_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_RaA_state],2)
	generic_IM_RaA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_RaA_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_RaA_state], generic_IM_RaA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_RaA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RaA_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_RaA_state],2)
	generic_IM_RaA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_RaA_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_RaA_state], generic_IM_RaA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_RaA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RaA_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_RaA_state],2)
	generic_IM_RaA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_RaA_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_RaA_state], generic_IM_RaA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Component Test Execution
	generic_IM_SCTE_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCTE_DevH_npt[2,generic_IM_SCTE_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCTE_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCTE_DevH_npt[1,generic_IM_SCTE_state], generic_IM_SCTE_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SCTE_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCTE_DevM_npt[2,generic_IM_SCTE_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCTE_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCTE_DevM_npt[1,generic_IM_SCTE_state], generic_IM_SCTE_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SCTE_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCTE_DevL_npt[2,generic_IM_SCTE_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCTE_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCTE_DevL_npt[1,generic_IM_SCTE_state], generic_IM_SCTE_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(Dev=H)P(attribute states|Dev=H)
	# m2 = P(Dev=M)P(attribute states|Dev=M)
	# m3 = P(Dev=L)P(attribute states|Dev=L)

	generic_IM_Dev_m1 <- IM_DevH_prior * generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevH_like * generic_IM_TA_DevH_like * generic_IM_CA_DevH_like * generic_IM_HA_DevH_like * generic_IM_SA_DevH_like * generic_IM_RA_DevH_like * generic_IM_CTCG_DevH_like * generic_IM_SITCG_DevH_like * generic_IM_SQTCG_DevH_like * generic_IM_SATCG_DevH_like * generic_IM_SCTPG_DevH_like * generic_IM_SITPG_DevH_like * generic_IM_SQTPG_DevH_like * generic_IM_CM_DevH_like * generic_IM_RaA_DevH_like * generic_IM_SCTE_DevH_like
	generic_IM_Dev_m2 <- IM_DevM_prior * generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevM_like * generic_IM_TA_DevM_like * generic_IM_CA_DevM_like * generic_IM_HA_DevM_like * generic_IM_SA_DevM_like * generic_IM_RA_DevM_like * generic_IM_CTCG_DevM_like * generic_IM_SITCG_DevM_like * generic_IM_SQTCG_DevM_like * generic_IM_SATCG_DevM_like * generic_IM_SCTPG_DevM_like * generic_IM_SITPG_DevM_like * generic_IM_SQTPG_DevM_like * generic_IM_CM_DevM_like * generic_IM_RaA_DevM_like * generic_IM_SCTE_DevM_like
	generic_IM_Dev_m3 <- IM_DevL_prior * generic_IM_SCaSCDG_DevL_like * generic_IM_TA_DevL_like * generic_IM_CA_DevL_like * generic_IM_HA_DevL_like * generic_IM_SA_DevL_like * generic_IM_RA_DevL_like * generic_IM_CTCG_DevL_like * generic_IM_SITCG_DevL_like * generic_IM_SQTCG_DevL_like * generic_IM_SATCG_DevL_like * generic_IM_SCTPG_DevL_like * generic_IM_SITPG_DevL_like * generic_IM_SQTPG_DevL_like * generic_IM_CM_DevL_like * generic_IM_RaA_DevL_like * generic_IM_SCTE_DevL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_IM_Dev_k <- 1 / (generic_IM_Dev_m1 + generic_IM_Dev_m2 + generic_IM_Dev_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in IM phase
	generic_IM_DevH_post <- generic_IM_Dev_k * generic_IM_Dev_m1
	generic_IM_DevM_post <- generic_IM_Dev_k * generic_IM_Dev_m2
	generic_IM_DevL_post <- generic_IM_Dev_k * generic_IM_Dev_m3


	# Generic V&V Attribute model - Implementation phase

	# Attribute Source Code and Source Code Documentation Evaluation

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCaSCDE_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_SCaSCDE_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of V&V quality)
	generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCaSCDE_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_SCaSCDE_state], generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCaSCDE_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_SCaSCDE_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCaSCDE_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_SCaSCDE_state], generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SCaSCDE_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_SCaSCDE_state],2)
	generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SCaSCDE_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_SCaSCDE_state], generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Interface Analysis V&V
	generic_IM_IAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_IAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_IAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_IAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_IAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_IAVV_state], generic_IM_IAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_IAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_IAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_IAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_IAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_IAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_IAVV_state], generic_IM_IAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_IAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_IAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_IAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_IAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_IAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_IAVV_state], generic_IM_IAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Traceability Analysis V&V
	generic_IM_TAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_TAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_TAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_TAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_TAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_TAVV_state], generic_IM_TAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_TAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_TAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_TAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_TAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_TAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_TAVV_state], generic_IM_TAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_TAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_TAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_TAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_TAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_TAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_TAVV_state], generic_IM_TAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Criticality Analysis V&V
	generic_IM_CAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_CAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_CAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_CAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_CAVV_state], generic_IM_CAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_CAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_CAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_CAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_CAVV_state], generic_IM_CAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_CAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_CAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_CAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_CAVV_state], generic_IM_CAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis V&V
	generic_IM_HAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_HAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_HAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_HAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_HAVV_state], generic_IM_HAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_HAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_HAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_HAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_HAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_HAVV_state], generic_IM_HAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_HAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_HAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_HAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_HAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_HAVV_state], generic_IM_HAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis V&V
	generic_IM_SAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_SAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_SAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_SAVV_state], generic_IM_SAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_SAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_SAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_SAVV_state], generic_IM_SAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_SAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_SAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_SAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_SAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_SAVV_state], generic_IM_SAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis V&V
	generic_IM_RAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_RAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_RAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_RAVV_state], generic_IM_RAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_RAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_RAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_RAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_RAVV_state], generic_IM_RAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_RAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_RAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_RAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_RAVV_state], generic_IM_RAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Component Test Case Generation
	generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSCTCG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSCTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSCTCG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSCTCG_state], generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSCTCG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSCTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSCTCG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSCTCG_state], generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSCTCG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSCTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSCTCG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSCTCG_state], generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Integration Test Case Generation
	generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSITCG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSITCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSITCG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSITCG_state], generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSITCG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSITCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSITCG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSITCG_state], generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSITCG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSITCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSITCG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSITCG_state], generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Quantification Test Case Generation
	generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSQTCG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSQTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSQTCG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSQTCG_state], generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSQTCG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSQTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSQTCG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSQTCG_state], generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSQTCG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSQTCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSQTCG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSQTCG_state], generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Acceptance Test Case Generation
	generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSATCG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSATCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSATCG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSATCG_state], generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSATCG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSATCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSATCG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSATCG_state], generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSATCG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSATCG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSATCG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSATCG_state], generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Component Test Procedure Generation
	generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSCTPG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSCTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSCTPG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSCTPG_state], generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSCTPG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSCTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSCTPG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSCTPG_state], generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSCTPG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSCTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSCTPG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSCTPG_state], generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Integration Test Procedure Generation
	generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSITPG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSITPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSITPG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSITPG_state], generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSITPG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSITPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSITPG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSITPG_state], generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSITPG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSITPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSITPG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSITPG_state], generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Quantification Test Procedure Generation
	generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSQTPG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSQTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSQTPG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSQTPG_state], generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSQTPG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSQTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSQTPG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSQTPG_state], generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSQTPG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSQTPG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSQTPG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSQTPG_state], generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Component Test Execution
	generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSCTE_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSCTE_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSCTE_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSCTE_state], generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSCTE_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSCTE_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSCTE_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSCTE_state], generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVSCTE_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_VVSCTE_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVSCTE_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_VVSCTE_state], generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Configuration Management V&V
	generic_IM_CMVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CMVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_CMVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_CMVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_CMVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_CMVV_state], generic_IM_CMVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CMVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CMVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_CMVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_CMVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_CMVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_CMVV_state], generic_IM_CMVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_CMVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_CMVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_CMVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_CMVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_CMVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_CMVV_state], generic_IM_CMVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Reviews and Audits V&V
	generic_IM_RaAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RaAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_RaAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_RaAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_RaAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_RaAVV_state], generic_IM_RaAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_RaAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RaAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_RaAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_RaAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_RaAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_RaAVV_state], generic_IM_RaAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_RaAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_RaAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_RaAVV_state],2)
	generic_IM_RaAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_RaAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_RaAVV_state], generic_IM_RaAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Implementation Phase Activity Summary Report Generation
	generic_IM_VVASRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVASRG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IM_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVASRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVASRG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IM_VVASRG_state], generic_IM_VVASRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVASRG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVASRG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IM_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVASRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVASRG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IM_VVASRG_state], generic_IM_VVASRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IM_VVASRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IM_VVASRG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IM_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_IM_VVASRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IM_VVASRG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IM_VVASRG_state], generic_IM_VVASRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(VV=H)P(attribute states|VV=H)
	# m2 = P(VV=M)P(attribute states|VV=M)
	# m3 = P(VV=L)P(attribute states|VV=L)

	generic_IM_VV_m1 <- IM_VVH_prior * generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVH_like * generic_IM_IAVV_VVH_like * generic_IM_TAVV_VVH_like * generic_IM_CAVV_VVH_like * generic_IM_HAVV_VVH_like * generic_IM_SAVV_VVH_like * generic_IM_RAVV_VVH_like * generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVH_like * generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVH_like * generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVH_like * generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVH_like * generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVH_like * generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVH_like * generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVH_like * generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVH_like * generic_IM_CMVV_VVH_like * generic_IM_RaAVV_VVH_like * generic_IM_VVASRG_VVH_like
	generic_IM_VV_m2 <- IM_VVM_prior * generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVM_like * generic_IM_IAVV_VVM_like * generic_IM_TAVV_VVM_like * generic_IM_CAVV_VVM_like * generic_IM_HAVV_VVM_like * generic_IM_SAVV_VVM_like * generic_IM_RAVV_VVM_like * generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVM_like * generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVM_like * generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVM_like * generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVM_like * generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVM_like * generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVM_like * generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVM_like * generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVM_like * generic_IM_CMVV_VVM_like * generic_IM_RaAVV_VVM_like * generic_IM_VVASRG_VVM_like
	generic_IM_VV_m3 <- IM_VVL_prior * generic_IM_SCaSCDE_VVL_like * generic_IM_IAVV_VVL_like * generic_IM_TAVV_VVL_like * generic_IM_CAVV_VVL_like * generic_IM_HAVV_VVL_like * generic_IM_SAVV_VVL_like * generic_IM_RAVV_VVL_like * generic_IM_VVSCTCG_VVL_like * generic_IM_VVSITCG_VVL_like * generic_IM_VVSQTCG_VVL_like * generic_IM_VVSATCG_VVL_like * generic_IM_VVSCTPG_VVL_like * generic_IM_VVSITPG_VVL_like * generic_IM_VVSQTPG_VVL_like * generic_IM_VVSCTE_VVL_like * generic_IM_CMVV_VVL_like * generic_IM_RaAVV_VVL_like * generic_IM_VVASRG_VVL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_IM_VV_k <- 1 / (generic_IM_VV_m1 + generic_IM_VV_m2 + generic_IM_VV_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in IM phase
	generic_IM_VVH_post <- generic_IM_VV_k * generic_IM_VV_m1
	generic_IM_VVM_post <- generic_IM_VV_k * generic_IM_VV_m2
	generic_IM_VVL_post <- generic_IM_VV_k * generic_IM_VV_m3


	# Generic Submodel - Implementation phase

	generic_IM_Defect_passed_from_SD <- generic_SD_Total_Remained_Defect

	# Defect density: the integral of P(Dev)*P(Defect Density|Dev) dDev
	generic_IM_Defect_Density <- (generic_IM_DevH_post * IM_DevH_DD_like + generic_IM_DevM_post * IM_DevM_DD_like + generic_IM_DevL_post * IM_DevL_DD_like)

	generic_IM_Defect_introduced_in_current <- generic_IM_FP * generic_IM_Defect_Density

	# Complexity: (FP >= 1000)? High: (FP >= 100)? Medium: Low
	generic_IM_Complexity <- step(generic_IM_FP-1000)+(1-step(generic_IM_FP-1000))*step(generic_IM_FP-100)*2+step(99-generic_IM_FP)*3

	# Defect Detection Probability (current) likelihood: P(DDP_current|state of VV quality)
	generic_IM_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_IM_Complexity],IM_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_IM_Complexity])
	generic_IM_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_IM_Complexity],IM_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_IM_Complexity])
	generic_IM_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_IM_Complexity],IM_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_IM_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (current): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	generic_IM_Defect_Detection_Probability_current <- generic_IM_VVH_post * generic_IM_VVH_DDP_current_like + generic_IM_VVM_post * generic_IM_VVM_DDP_current_like + generic_IM_VVL_post * generic_IM_VVL_DDP_current_like

	generic_IM_Detected_Defect_current <- generic_IM_Defect_introduced_in_current * generic_IM_Defect_Detection_Probability_current

	generic_IM_Remaining_Defect_current <- generic_IM_Defect_introduced_in_current - generic_IM_Detected_Defect_current

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous) likelihood: P(DDP_previous|state of VV quality)
	generic_IM_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_IM_Complexity],IM_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_IM_Complexity])
	generic_IM_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_IM_Complexity],IM_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_IM_Complexity])
	generic_IM_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IM_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_IM_Complexity],IM_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_IM_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	generic_IM_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous <- generic_IM_VVH_post * generic_IM_VVH_DDP_previous_like + generic_IM_VVM_post * generic_IM_VVM_DDP_previous_like + generic_IM_VVL_post * generic_IM_VVL_DDP_previous_like

	generic_IM_Detected_Defect_previous <- generic_IM_Defect_passed_from_SD * generic_IM_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous

	generic_IM_Remaining_Defect_previous <- generic_IM_Defect_passed_from_SD - generic_IM_Detected_Defect_previous

	generic_IM_Total_Remained_Defect <- generic_IM_Remaining_Defect_current + generic_IM_Remaining_Defect_previous


	# Generic Dev Attribute model - Test phase

	# Attribute Software Integration Test Execution

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_ST_SITE_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SITE_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_SITE_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of Dev quality)
	generic_ST_SITE_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SITE_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_SITE_state], generic_ST_SITE_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_SITE_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SITE_DevM_npt[2,generic_ST_SITE_state],2)
	generic_ST_SITE_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SITE_DevM_npt[1,generic_ST_SITE_state], generic_ST_SITE_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_SITE_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SITE_DevL_npt[2,generic_ST_SITE_state],2)
	generic_ST_SITE_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SITE_DevL_npt[1,generic_ST_SITE_state], generic_ST_SITE_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Qualification Test Execution
	generic_ST_SQTE_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SQTE_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_SQTE_state],2)
	generic_ST_SQTE_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SQTE_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_SQTE_state], generic_ST_SQTE_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_SQTE_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SQTE_DevM_npt[2,generic_ST_SQTE_state],2)
	generic_ST_SQTE_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SQTE_DevM_npt[1,generic_ST_SQTE_state], generic_ST_SQTE_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_SQTE_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SQTE_DevL_npt[2,generic_ST_SQTE_state],2)
	generic_ST_SQTE_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SQTE_DevL_npt[1,generic_ST_SQTE_state], generic_ST_SQTE_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Acceptance Procedure Generation
	generic_ST_SAPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SAPG_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_SAPG_state],2)
	generic_ST_SAPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SAPG_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_SAPG_state], generic_ST_SAPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_SAPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SAPG_DevM_npt[2,generic_ST_SAPG_state],2)
	generic_ST_SAPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SAPG_DevM_npt[1,generic_ST_SAPG_state], generic_ST_SAPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_SAPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SAPG_DevL_npt[2,generic_ST_SAPG_state],2)
	generic_ST_SAPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SAPG_DevL_npt[1,generic_ST_SAPG_state], generic_ST_SAPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Software Acceptance Test Execution
	generic_ST_SATE_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SATE_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_SATE_state],2)
	generic_ST_SATE_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SATE_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_SATE_state], generic_ST_SATE_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_SATE_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SATE_DevM_npt[2,generic_ST_SATE_state],2)
	generic_ST_SATE_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_SATE_DevM_npt[1,generic_ST_SATE_state], generic_ST_SATE_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_SATE_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SATE_DevL_npt[2,generic_ST_SATE_state],2)
	generic_ST_SATE_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SATE_DevL_npt[1,generic_ST_SATE_state], generic_ST_SATE_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Traceability Analysis - Test Phase
	generic_ST_TA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_TA_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_TA_state],2)
	generic_ST_TA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_TA_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_TA_state], generic_ST_TA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_TA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_TA_DevM_npt[2,generic_ST_TA_state],2)
	generic_ST_TA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_TA_DevM_npt[1,generic_ST_TA_state], generic_ST_TA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_TA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_TA_DevL_npt[2,generic_ST_TA_state],2)
	generic_ST_TA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_TA_DevL_npt[1,generic_ST_TA_state], generic_ST_TA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis - Test Phase
	generic_ST_HA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_HA_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_HA_state],2)
	generic_ST_HA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_HA_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_HA_state], generic_ST_HA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_HA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_HA_DevM_npt[2,generic_ST_HA_state],2)
	generic_ST_HA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_HA_DevM_npt[1,generic_ST_HA_state], generic_ST_HA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_HA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_HA_DevL_npt[2,generic_ST_HA_state],2)
	generic_ST_HA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_HA_DevL_npt[1,generic_ST_HA_state], generic_ST_HA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis - Test Phase
	generic_ST_SA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SA_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_SA_state],2)
	generic_ST_SA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_SA_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_SA_state], generic_ST_SA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_SA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SA_DevM_npt[2,generic_ST_SA_state],2)

	generic_ST_SA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_SA_DevL_npt[2,generic_ST_SA_state],2)
	generic_ST_SA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_SA_DevL_npt[1,generic_ST_SA_state], generic_ST_SA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis - Test Phase
	generic_ST_RA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RA_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_RA_state],2)
	generic_ST_RA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_RA_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_RA_state], generic_ST_RA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Configuration Management
	generic_ST_CM_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_CM_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_CM_state],2)
	generic_ST_CM_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_CM_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_CM_state], generic_ST_CM_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_CM_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_CM_DevM_npt[2,generic_ST_CM_state],2)
	generic_ST_CM_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_CM_DevM_npt[1,generic_ST_CM_state], generic_ST_CM_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_CM_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_CM_DevL_npt[2,generic_ST_CM_state],2)
	generic_ST_CM_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_CM_DevL_npt[1,generic_ST_CM_state], generic_ST_CM_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Review and Audits
	generic_ST_RaA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaA_DevH_npt[2,generic_ST_RaA_state],2)
	generic_ST_RaA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(ST_RaA_DevH_npt[1,generic_ST_RaA_state], generic_ST_RaA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_RaA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaA_DevM_npt[2,generic_ST_RaA_state],2)
	generic_ST_RaA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(ST_RaA_DevM_npt[1,generic_ST_RaA_state], generic_ST_RaA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_RaA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaA_DevL_npt[2,generic_ST_RaA_state],2)
	generic_ST_RaA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(ST_RaA_DevL_npt[1,generic_ST_RaA_state], generic_ST_RaA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(Dev=H)P(attribute states|Dev=H)
	# m2 = P(Dev=M)P(attribute states|Dev=M)
	# m3 = P(Dev=L)P(attribute states|Dev=L)

	generic_ST_Dev_m1 <- ST_DevH_prior * generic_ST_SITE_DevH_like * generic_ST_SQTE_DevH_like * generic_ST_SAPG_DevH_like * generic_ST_SATE_DevH_like * generic_ST_TA_DevH_like * generic_ST_HA_DevH_like * generic_ST_SA_DevH_like * generic_ST_RA_DevH_like * generic_ST_CM_DevH_like * generic_ST_RaA_DevH_like
	generic_ST_Dev_m2 <- ST_DevM_prior * generic_ST_SITE_DevM_like * generic_ST_SQTE_DevM_like * generic_ST_SAPG_DevM_like * generic_ST_SATE_DevM_like * generic_ST_TA_DevM_like * generic_ST_HA_DevM_like * generic_ST_SA_DevM_like * generic_ST_RA_DevM_like * generic_ST_CM_DevM_like * generic_ST_RaA_DevM_like
	generic_ST_Dev_m3 <- ST_DevL_prior * generic_ST_SITE_DevL_like * generic_ST_SQTE_DevL_like * generic_ST_SAPG_DevL_like * generic_ST_SATE_DevL_like * generic_ST_TA_DevL_like * generic_ST_HA_DevL_like * generic_ST_SA_DevL_like * generic_ST_RA_DevL_like * generic_ST_CM_DevL_like * generic_ST_RaA_DevL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_ST_Dev_k <- 1 / (generic_ST_Dev_m1 + generic_ST_Dev_m2 + generic_ST_Dev_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in ST phase
	generic_ST_DevH_post <- generic_ST_Dev_k * generic_ST_Dev_m1
	generic_ST_DevM_post <- generic_ST_Dev_k * generic_ST_Dev_m2
	generic_ST_DevL_post <- generic_ST_Dev_k * generic_ST_Dev_m3


	# Generic V&V Attribute model - Test phase

	# Attribute V&V Software Integration Test Execution

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_ST_VVSITE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSITE_VVH_npt[2,generic_ST_VVSITE_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of V&V quality)
	generic_ST_VVSITE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSITE_VVH_npt[1,generic_ST_VVSITE_state], generic_ST_VVSITE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_VVSITE_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSITE_VVM_npt[2,generic_ST_VVSITE_state],2)
	generic_ST_VVSITE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSITE_VVM_npt[1,generic_ST_VVSITE_state], generic_ST_VVSITE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_VVSITE_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSITE_VVL_npt[2,generic_ST_VVSITE_state],2)
	generic_ST_VVSITE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSITE_VVL_npt[1,generic_ST_VVSITE_state], generic_ST_VVSITE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Qualification Test Execution
	generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSQTE_VVH_npt[2,generic_ST_VVSQTE_state],2)
	generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSQTE_VVH_npt[1,generic_ST_VVSQTE_state], generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSQTE_VVM_npt[1,generic_ST_VVSQTE_state], generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSQTE_VVL_npt[1,generic_ST_VVSQTE_state], generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Software Acceptance Procedure Generation
	generic_ST_VVSAPG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVSAPG_VVH_npt[2,generic_ST_VVSAPG_state],2)
	generic_ST_VVSAPG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVSAPG_VVH_npt[1,generic_ST_VVSAPG_state], generic_ST_VVSAPG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_RaAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_RaAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_ST_RaAVV_state],2)

	# Attribute V&V Test phase Activity Summary Report Generation
	generic_ST_VVASRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVASRG_VVH_npt[2,generic_ST_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_ST_VVASRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVASRG_VVH_npt[1,generic_ST_VVASRG_state], generic_ST_VVASRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_VVASRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVASRG_VVM_npt[1,generic_ST_VVASRG_state], generic_ST_VVASRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_ST_VVASRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(ST_VVASRG_VVL_npt[2,generic_ST_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_ST_VVASRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(ST_VVASRG_VVL_npt[1,generic_ST_VVASRG_state], generic_ST_VVASRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(VV=H)P(attribute states|VV=H)
	# m2 = P(VV=M)P(attribute states|VV=M)
	# m3 = P(VV=L)P(attribute states|VV=L)

	generic_ST_VV_m1 <- ST_VVH_prior * generic_ST_VVSITE_VVH_like * generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVH_like * generic_ST_VVSAPG_VVH_like * generic_ST_VVSATE_VVH_like * generic_ST_TAVV_VVH_like * generic_ST_HAVV_VVH_like * generic_ST_SAVV_VVH_like * generic_ST_RAVV_VVH_like * generic_ST_CMVV_VVH_like * generic_ST_RaAVV_VVH_like * generic_ST_VVASRG_VVH_like
	generic_ST_VV_m2 <- ST_VVM_prior * generic_ST_VVSITE_VVM_like * generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVM_like * generic_ST_VVSAPG_VVM_like * generic_ST_VVSATE_VVM_like * generic_ST_TAVV_VVM_like * generic_ST_HAVV_VVM_like * generic_ST_SAVV_VVM_like * generic_ST_RAVV_VVM_like * generic_ST_CMVV_VVM_like * generic_ST_RaAVV_VVM_like * generic_ST_VVASRG_VVM_like
	generic_ST_VV_m3 <- ST_VVL_prior * generic_ST_VVSITE_VVL_like * generic_ST_VVSQTE_VVL_like * generic_ST_VVSAPG_VVL_like * generic_ST_VVSATE_VVL_like * generic_ST_TAVV_VVL_like * generic_ST_HAVV_VVL_like * generic_ST_SAVV_VVL_like * generic_ST_RAVV_VVL_like * generic_ST_CMVV_VVL_like * generic_ST_RaAVV_VVL_like * generic_ST_VVASRG_VVL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_ST_VV_k <- 1 / (generic_ST_VV_m1 + generic_ST_VV_m2 + generic_ST_VV_m3)

	# posterior probability of V&V quality in ST phase
	generic_ST_VVH_post <- generic_ST_VV_k * generic_ST_VV_m1
	generic_ST_VVM_post <- generic_ST_VV_k * generic_ST_VV_m2
	generic_ST_VVL_post <- generic_ST_VV_k * generic_ST_VV_m3


	# Generic Submodel - Test phase

	generic_ST_Defect_passed_from_IM <- generic_IM_Total_Remained_Defect

	# Defect density: the integral of P(Dev)*P(Defect Density|Dev) dDev
	generic_ST_Defect_Density <- (generic_ST_DevH_post * ST_DevH_DD_like + generic_ST_DevM_post * ST_DevM_DD_like + generic_ST_DevL_post * ST_DevL_DD_like)

	generic_ST_Defect_introduced_in_current <- generic_ST_FP * generic_ST_Defect_Density

	# Complexity: (FP >= 1000)? High: (FP >= 100)? Medium: Low
	generic_ST_Complexity <- step(generic_ST_FP-1000)+(1-step(generic_ST_FP-1000))*step(generic_ST_FP-100)*2+step(99-generic_ST_FP)*3

	# Defect Detection Probability (current) likelihood: P(DDP_current|state of Dev quality, state of VV quality)
	generic_ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (current): the integral of P(DDP_current|Dev, VV) dDev,VV
	generic_ST_Defect_Detection_Probability_current <- generic_ST_DevH_post * generic_ST_VVH_post * generic_ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_current_like + generic_ST_DevH_post * generic_ST_VVM_post * generic_ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_current_like + generic_ST_DevH_post * generic_ST_VVL_post * generic_ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_current_like + generic_ST_DevM_post * generic_ST_VVH_post * generic_ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_current_like + generic_ST_DevM_post * generic_ST_VVM_post * generic_ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_current_like + generic_ST_DevM_post * generic_ST_VVL_post * generic_ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_current_like + generic_ST_DevL_post * generic_ST_VVH_post * generic_ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_current_like + generic_ST_DevL_post * generic_ST_VVM_post * generic_ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_current_like + generic_ST_DevL_post * generic_ST_VVL_post * generic_ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_current_like

	generic_ST_Detected_Defect_current <- generic_ST_Defect_introduced_in_current * generic_ST_Defect_Detection_Probability_current

	generic_ST_Remaining_Defect_current <- generic_ST_Defect_introduced_in_current - generic_ST_Detected_Defect_current

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous) likelihood: P(DDP_previous|state of Dev quality, state of VV quality)
	generic_ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])
	generic_ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_ST_Complexity],ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_ST_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous): the integral of P(DDP_previous|Dev, VV) dDev,VV
	generic_ST_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous <- generic_ST_DevH_post * generic_ST_VVH_post * generic_ST_DevH_VVH_DDP_previous_like + generic_ST_DevH_post * generic_ST_VVM_post * generic_ST_DevH_VVM_DDP_previous_like + generic_ST_DevH_post * generic_ST_VVL_post * generic_ST_DevH_VVL_DDP_previous_like + generic_ST_DevM_post * generic_ST_VVH_post * generic_ST_DevM_VVH_DDP_previous_like + generic_ST_DevM_post * generic_ST_VVM_post * generic_ST_DevM_VVM_DDP_previous_like + generic_ST_DevM_post * generic_ST_VVL_post * generic_ST_DevM_VVL_DDP_previous_like + generic_ST_DevL_post * generic_ST_VVH_post * generic_ST_DevL_VVH_DDP_previous_like + generic_ST_DevL_post * generic_ST_VVM_post * generic_ST_DevL_VVM_DDP_previous_like + generic_ST_DevL_post * generic_ST_VVL_post * generic_ST_DevL_VVL_DDP_previous_like

	generic_ST_Detected_Defect_previous <- generic_ST_Defect_passed_from_IM * generic_ST_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous

	generic_ST_Remaining_Defect_previous <- generic_ST_Defect_passed_from_IM - generic_ST_Detected_Defect_previous

	generic_ST_Total_Remained_Defect <- generic_ST_Remaining_Defect_current + generic_ST_Remaining_Defect_previous


	# Generic Dev Attribute model - Installation & Checkout phase

	# Attribute Installation Procedure Generation

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_IC_IPG_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IPG_DevH_npt[2,generic_IC_IPG_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of Dev quality)
	generic_IC_IPG_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_IPG_DevH_npt[1,generic_IC_IPG_state], generic_IC_IPG_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_IPG_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IPG_DevM_npt[2,generic_IC_IPG_state],2)
	generic_IC_IPG_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_IPG_DevM_npt[1,generic_IC_IPG_state], generic_IC_IPG_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_IPG_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IPG_DevL_npt[2,generic_IC_IPG_state],2)
	generic_IC_IPG_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_IPG_DevL_npt[1,generic_IC_IPG_state], generic_IC_IPG_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Installation and Checkout
	generic_IC_IaC_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IaC_DevH_npt[2,generic_IC_IaC_state],2)
	generic_IC_IaC_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_IaC_DevH_npt[1,generic_IC_IaC_state], generic_IC_IaC_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_IaC_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IaC_DevM_npt[2,generic_IC_IaC_state],2)
	generic_IC_IaC_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_IaC_DevM_npt[1,generic_IC_IaC_state], generic_IC_IaC_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_IaC_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_IaC_DevL_npt[2,generic_IC_IaC_state],2)
	generic_IC_IaC_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_IaC_DevL_npt[1,generic_IC_IaC_state], generic_IC_IaC_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis - IC phase
	generic_IC_HA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HA_DevH_npt[2,generic_IC_HA_state],2)
	generic_IC_HA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_HA_DevH_npt[1,generic_IC_HA_state], generic_IC_HA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_HA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HA_DevM_npt[2,generic_IC_HA_state],2)
	generic_IC_HA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_HA_DevM_npt[1,generic_IC_HA_state], generic_IC_HA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_HA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HA_DevL_npt[2,generic_IC_HA_state],2)
	generic_IC_HA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_HA_DevL_npt[1,generic_IC_HA_state], generic_IC_HA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis - IC phase
	generic_IC_SA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SA_DevH_npt[2,generic_IC_SA_state],2)
	generic_IC_SA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_SA_DevH_npt[1,generic_IC_SA_state], generic_IC_SA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_SA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SA_DevM_npt[2,generic_IC_SA_state],2)
	generic_IC_SA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_SA_DevM_npt[1,generic_IC_SA_state], generic_IC_SA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_SA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SA_DevL_npt[2,generic_IC_SA_state],2)
	generic_IC_SA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_SA_DevL_npt[1,generic_IC_SA_state], generic_IC_SA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis - IC phase
	generic_IC_RA_DevH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RA_DevH_npt[2,generic_IC_RA_state],2)
	generic_IC_RA_DevH_like ~ dnorm(IC_RA_DevH_npt[1,generic_IC_RA_state], generic_IC_RA_DevH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_RA_DevM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RA_DevM_npt[2,generic_IC_RA_state],2)
	generic_IC_RA_DevM_like ~ dnorm(IC_RA_DevM_npt[1,generic_IC_RA_state], generic_IC_RA_DevM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_RA_DevL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RA_DevL_npt[2,generic_IC_RA_state],2)
	generic_IC_RA_DevL_like ~ dnorm(IC_RA_DevL_npt[1,generic_IC_RA_state], generic_IC_RA_DevL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(Dev=H)P(attribute states|Dev=H)
	# m2 = P(Dev=M)P(attribute states|Dev=M)
	# m3 = P(Dev=L)P(attribute states|Dev=L)

	generic_IC_Dev_m1 <- IC_DevH_prior * generic_IC_IPG_DevH_like * generic_IC_IaC_DevH_like * generic_IC_HA_DevH_like * generic_IC_SA_DevH_like * generic_IC_RA_DevH_like
	generic_IC_Dev_m2 <- IC_DevM_prior * generic_IC_IPG_DevM_like * generic_IC_IaC_DevM_like * generic_IC_HA_DevM_like * generic_IC_SA_DevM_like * generic_IC_RA_DevM_like
	generic_IC_Dev_m3 <- IC_DevL_prior * generic_IC_IPG_DevL_like * generic_IC_IaC_DevL_like * generic_IC_HA_DevL_like * generic_IC_SA_DevL_like * generic_IC_RA_DevL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_IC_Dev_k <- 1 / (generic_IC_Dev_m1 + generic_IC_Dev_m2 + generic_IC_Dev_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in IC phase
	generic_IC_DevH_post <- generic_IC_Dev_k * generic_IC_Dev_m1
	generic_IC_DevM_post <- generic_IC_Dev_k * generic_IC_Dev_m2
	generic_IC_DevL_post <- generic_IC_Dev_k * generic_IC_Dev_m3


	# Generic V&V Attribute model - Installation & Checkout phase

	# Attribute Installation Configuration Audit V&V

	# tau: precision parameter of normal distribution (tau = 1/(sigma^2))
	generic_IC_ICAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IC_ICAVV_state],2)

	# likelihood: conditional probability P(attribute state|state of V&V quality)
	generic_IC_ICAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IC_ICAVV_state], generic_IC_ICAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_ICAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IC_ICAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_ICAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IC_ICAVV_state], generic_IC_ICAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_ICAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IC_ICAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_ICAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IC_ICAVV_state], generic_IC_ICAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Installation Checkout V&V
	generic_IC_ICVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IC_ICVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_ICVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IC_ICVV_state], generic_IC_ICVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_ICVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IC_ICVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_ICVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IC_ICVV_state], generic_IC_ICVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_ICVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_ICVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IC_ICVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_ICVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_ICVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IC_ICVV_state], generic_IC_ICVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Hazard Analysis V&V
	generic_IC_HAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IC_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_HAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_HAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IC_HAVV_state], generic_IC_HAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_HAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IC_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_HAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_HAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IC_HAVV_state], generic_IC_HAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_HAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_HAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IC_HAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_HAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_HAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IC_HAVV_state], generic_IC_HAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Security Analysis V&V
	generic_IC_SAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IC_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_SAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_SAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IC_SAVV_state], generic_IC_SAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_SAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IC_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_SAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_SAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IC_SAVV_state], generic_IC_SAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_SAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_SAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IC_SAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_SAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_SAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IC_SAVV_state], generic_IC_SAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute Risk Analysis V&V
	generic_IC_RAVV_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RAVV_VVH_npt[2,generic_IC_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_RAVV_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_RAVV_VVH_npt[1,generic_IC_RAVV_state], generic_IC_RAVV_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_RAVV_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RAVV_VVM_npt[2,generic_IC_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_RAVV_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_RAVV_VVM_npt[1,generic_IC_RAVV_state], generic_IC_RAVV_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_RAVV_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_RAVV_VVL_npt[2,generic_IC_RAVV_state],2)
	generic_IC_RAVV_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_RAVV_VVL_npt[1,generic_IC_RAVV_state], generic_IC_RAVV_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Installation and Checkout Phase Activity Summary Report Generation
	generic_IC_VVASRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVASRG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IC_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_IC_VVASRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVASRG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IC_VVASRG_state], generic_IC_VVASRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_VVASRG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVASRG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IC_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_IC_VVASRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVASRG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IC_VVASRG_state], generic_IC_VVASRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_VVASRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVASRG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IC_VVASRG_state],2)
	generic_IC_VVASRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVASRG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IC_VVASRG_state], generic_IC_VVASRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# Attribute V&V Final Report Generation
	generic_IC_VVFRG_VVH_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVFRG_VVH_npt[2,generic_IC_VVFRG_state],2)
	generic_IC_VVFRG_VVH_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVFRG_VVH_npt[1,generic_IC_VVFRG_state], generic_IC_VVFRG_VVH_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_VVFRG_VVM_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVFRG_VVM_npt[2,generic_IC_VVFRG_state],2)
	generic_IC_VVFRG_VVM_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVFRG_VVM_npt[1,generic_IC_VVFRG_state], generic_IC_VVFRG_VVM_tau)I(0,1)

	generic_IC_VVFRG_VVL_tau <- 1 / pow(IC_VVFRG_VVL_npt[2,generic_IC_VVFRG_state],2)
	generic_IC_VVFRG_VVL_like ~ dnorm(IC_VVFRG_VVL_npt[1,generic_IC_VVFRG_state], generic_IC_VVFRG_VVL_tau)I(0,1)

	# m1-m3: a part of marginal probability
	# m1 = P(VV=H)P(attribute states|VV=H)
	# m2 = P(VV=M)P(attribute states|VV=M)
	# m3 = P(VV=L)P(attribute states|VV=L)

	generic_IC_VV_m1 <- IC_VVH_prior * generic_IC_ICAVV_VVH_like * generic_IC_ICVV_VVH_like * generic_IC_HAVV_VVH_like * generic_IC_SAVV_VVH_like * generic_IC_RAVV_VVH_like * generic_IC_VVASRG_VVH_like * generic_IC_VVFRG_VVH_like
	generic_IC_VV_m2 <- IC_VVM_prior * generic_IC_ICAVV_VVM_like * generic_IC_ICVV_VVM_like * generic_IC_HAVV_VVM_like * generic_IC_SAVV_VVM_like * generic_IC_RAVV_VVM_like * generic_IC_VVASRG_VVM_like * generic_IC_VVFRG_VVM_like
	generic_IC_VV_m3 <- IC_VVL_prior * generic_IC_ICAVV_VVL_like * generic_IC_ICVV_VVL_like * generic_IC_HAVV_VVL_like * generic_IC_SAVV_VVL_like * generic_IC_RAVV_VVL_like * generic_IC_VVASRG_VVL_like * generic_IC_VVFRG_VVL_like

	# k = 1 / marginal probability
	generic_IC_VV_k <- 1 / (generic_IC_VV_m1 + generic_IC_VV_m2 + generic_IC_VV_m3)

	# posterior probability of Dev quality in IC phase
	generic_IC_VVH_post <- generic_IC_VV_k * generic_IC_VV_m1
	generic_IC_VVM_post <- generic_IC_VV_k * generic_IC_VV_m2
	generic_IC_VVL_post <- generic_IC_VV_k * generic_IC_VV_m3


	# Generic Submodel - Installation & Checkout phase

	generic_IC_Defect_passed_from_ST <- generic_ST_Total_Remained_Defect

	# Defect density: the integral of P(Dev)*P(Defect Density|Dev) dDev
	generic_IC_Defect_Density <- (generic_IC_DevH_post * IC_DevH_DD_like + generic_IC_DevM_post * IC_DevM_DD_like + generic_IC_DevL_post * IC_DevL_DD_like)

	generic_IC_Defect_introduced_in_current <- generic_IC_FP * generic_IC_Defect_Density

	# Complexity: (FP >= 1000)? High: (FP >= 100)? Medium: Low
	generic_IC_Complexity <- step(generic_IC_FP-1000)+(1-step(generic_IC_FP-1000))*step(generic_IC_FP-100)*2+step(99-generic_IC_FP)*3

	# Defect Detection Probability (current) likelihood: P(DDP_current|state of VV quality)
	generic_IC_VVH_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVH_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_IC_Complexity],IC_VVH_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_IC_Complexity])
	generic_IC_VVM_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVM_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_IC_Complexity],IC_VVM_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_IC_Complexity])
	generic_IC_VVL_DDP_current_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVL_DDP_current_npt[1,generic_IC_Complexity],IC_VVL_DDP_current_npt[2,generic_IC_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (current): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	generic_IC_Defect_Detection_Probability_current <- generic_IC_VVH_post * generic_IC_VVH_DDP_current_like + generic_IC_VVM_post * generic_IC_VVM_DDP_current_like + generic_IC_VVL_post * generic_IC_VVL_DDP_current_like

	generic_IC_Detected_Defect_current <- generic_IC_Defect_introduced_in_current * generic_IC_Defect_Detection_Probability_current

	generic_IC_Remaining_Defect_current <- generic_IC_Defect_introduced_in_current - generic_IC_Detected_Defect_current

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous) likelihood: P(DDP_previous|state of VV quality)
	generic_IC_VVH_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_IC_Complexity],IC_VVH_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_IC_Complexity])
	generic_IC_VVM_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_IC_Complexity],IC_VVM_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_IC_Complexity])
	generic_IC_VVL_DDP_previous_like ~ dbeta(IC_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[1,generic_IC_Complexity],IC_VVL_DDP_previous_npt[2,generic_IC_Complexity])

	# Defect Detection Probability (previous): the integral of P(DDP_current|VV) dVV
	generic_IC_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous <- generic_IC_VVH_post * generic_IC_VVH_DDP_previous_like + generic_IC_VVM_post * generic_IC_VVM_DDP_previous_like + generic_IC_VVL_post * generic_IC_VVL_DDP_previous_like

	generic_IC_Detected_Defect_previous <- generic_IC_Defect_passed_from_ST * generic_IC_Defect_Detection_Probability_previous

	generic_IC_Remaining_Defect_previous <- generic_IC_Defect_passed_from_ST - generic_IC_Detected_Defect_previous

	generic_IC_Total_Remained_Defect <- generic_IC_Remaining_Defect_current + generic_IC_Remaining_Defect_previous

	generic_SFP_tau <- 1 / pow(2.217,2)
	generic_SFP ~ dlnorm(-10.45, generic_SFP_tau)

	generic_FSD <- generic_SFP / generic_IC_Total_Remained_Defect




	#### PFD estimation ####
	PFD <- generic_FSD * IC_Total_Remained_Defect
}
